I've uploaded a code repository in the directory . Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
[BUG] nacos v3 api 和 grpc客户端机制不一致
  gRPC 和 v3 HTTP 的核心差异对比：

  gRPC 路径（正常）

  ServiceQueryRequestHandler.handle()
    cluster = request.getCluster() == null ? "" : request.getCluster()  // 空串
    → ServiceUtil.doSelectInstances(serviceInfo, "", ...)
    → clusterSets = StringUtils.isNotBlank("") ? ... : new HashSet<>()  // 空 Set
    → checkCluster(空Set, instance) → clusterSets.isEmpty() → return true  // 全部通过

  v3 HTTP 路径（有问题）

  InstanceListForm.fillDefaultValue()
    clusterName 为空 → 填充为 "DEFAULT"               // 强制覆盖
    → CatalogServiceV2Impl.listInstances(..., "DEFAULT")
    → serviceStorage.getClusters(service).contains("DEFAULT")  // false，cluster-hba ≠ DEFAULT
    → throw NacosException NOT_FOUND → controller 返回空 data


  结论： 两套路径用了完全不同的实现。gRPC 走 ServiceUtil.doSelectInstances，空 cluster 时 clusterSets 为空 Set，checkCluster 直接返回 true 放行所有实例。v3 HTTP 走
  CatalogServiceV2Impl.listInstances，InstanceListForm.fillDefaultValue() 把空 cluster 强制填成 "DEFAULT"，然后做精确匹配，找不到就抛异常。

  这是 v3 HTTP API 新增时没有复用 ServiceUtil 的过滤逻辑，导致行为不一致，属于 Bug。修复方式是 InstanceListForm.fillDefaultValue() 不应该对 clusterName
  做默认填充，或者 listInstances 里 clusterName 为空时走 listAllInstances 的逻辑。

</pr_description>

    53	    public void validate() throws NacosApiException {

    57	                    "Required parameter 'serviceName' type String is not present");
    58	        }
    59	    }
    60	    
    61	    /**
    62	     * fill default value.
    63	     */
    64	    public void fillDefaultValue() {
    65	        if (StringUtils.isBlank(namespaceId)) {
    66	            namespaceId = Constants.DEFAULT_NAMESPACE_ID;
    67	        }
    68	        if (StringUtils.isBlank(groupName)) {
    69	            groupName = Constants.DEFAULT_GROUP;
    70	        }
    71	        if (StringUtils.isBlank(clusterName)) {
    72	            clusterName = UtilsAndCommons.DEFAULT_CLUSTER_NAME;
    73	        }
    74	        if (null == healthyOnly) {
    75	            healthyOnly = false;
    76	        }
    77	    }

   119	    @Override
   120	    public boolean equals(Object o) {
   121	        if (this == o) {
   122	            return true;
   123	        }
   124	        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass()) {
   125	            return false;
   126	        }
   127	        InstanceListForm that = (InstanceListForm) o;
   128	        return Objects.equals(namespaceId, that.namespaceId) && Objects.equals(groupName, that.groupName)
   129	                && Objects.equals(serviceName, that.serviceName) && Objects.equals(clusterName, that.clusterName)
   130	                && Objects.equals(healthyOnly, that.healthyOnly);
   131	    }

    17	package com.alibaba.nacos.naming.core;
    18	
    19	import com.alibaba.nacos.api.common.Constants;
    20	import com.alibaba.nacos.api.exception.NacosException;
    21	import com.alibaba.nacos.api.model.Page;
    22	import com.alibaba.nacos.api.naming.pojo.Instance;
    23	import com.alibaba.nacos.api.naming.pojo.ServiceInfo;
    24	import com.alibaba.nacos.api.naming.pojo.maintainer.ClusterInfo;
    25	import com.alibaba.nacos.api.naming.pojo.maintainer.ServiceDetailInfo;
    26	import com.alibaba.nacos.api.naming.pojo.maintainer.ServiceView;
    27	import com.alibaba.nacos.common.utils.JacksonUtils;
    28	import com.alibaba.nacos.common.utils.StringUtils;
    29	import com.alibaba.nacos.core.utils.PageUtil;
    30	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.constants.FieldsConstants;
    31	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.core.v2.ServiceManager;
    32	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.core.v2.index.ServiceStorage;
    33	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.core.v2.metadata.ClusterMetadata;
    34	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.core.v2.metadata.NamingMetadataManager;
    35	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.core.v2.metadata.ServiceMetadata;
    36	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.core.v2.pojo.Service;
    37	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.utils.ServiceUtil;
    38	import com.fasterxml.jackson.databind.node.ObjectNode;
    39	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
    40	
    41	import java.util.Collection;
    42	import java.util.Collections;
    43	import java.util.HashMap;
    44	import java.util.LinkedList;
    45	import java.util.List;
    46	import java.util.Map;
    47	import java.util.Optional;
    48	import java.util.StringJoiner;
    49	import java.util.stream.Collectors;
    50	
    51	/**
    52	 * Catalog service for v2.x .
    53	 *
    54	 * @author xiweng.yy
    55	 */
    56	@Component()
    57	public class CatalogServiceV2Impl implements CatalogService {
    58	    
    59	    private final ServiceStorage serviceStorage;
    60	    
    61	    private final NamingMetadataManager metadataManager;
    62	    
    63	    private static final int DEFAULT_PORT = 80;
    64	    
    65	    public CatalogServiceV2Impl(ServiceStorage serviceStorage, NamingMetadataManager metadataManager) {
    66	        this.serviceStorage = serviceStorage;
    67	        this.metadataManager = metadataManager;
    68	    }
    69	    
    70	    @Override
    71	    public ServiceDetailInfo getServiceDetail(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName)
    72	            throws NacosException {
    73	        Service service = Service.newService(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName);
    74	        if (!ServiceManager.getInstance().containSingleton(service)) {
    75	            throw new NacosException(NacosException.NOT_FOUND,
    76	                    String.format("service %s@@%s is not found!", groupName, serviceName));
    77	        }
    78	        service = ServiceManager.getInstance().getSingleton(service);
    79	        Optional<ServiceMetadata> metadata = metadataManager.getServiceMetadata(service);
    80	        ServiceMetadata detailedService = metadata.orElseGet(ServiceMetadata::new);
    81	        
    82	        ServiceDetailInfo result = new ServiceDetailInfo();
    83	        result.setNamespaceId(service.getNamespace());
    84	        result.setGroupName(service.getGroup());
    85	        result.setServiceName(serviceName);
    86	        result.setEphemeral(service.isEphemeral());
    87	        result.setProtectThreshold(detailedService.getProtectThreshold());
    88	        result.setSelector(detailedService.getSelector());
    89	        result.setMetadata(detailedService.getExtendData());
    90	        
    91	        Map<String, ClusterInfo> clusters = new HashMap<>(serviceStorage.getClusters(service).size());
    92	        for (String each : serviceStorage.getClusters(service)) {
    93	            ClusterMetadata clusterMetadata =
    94	                    detailedService.getClusters().containsKey(each) ? detailedService.getClusters().get(each)
    95	                            : new ClusterMetadata();
    96	            ClusterInfo clusterInfo = new ClusterInfo();
    97	            clusterInfo.setClusterName(each);
    98	            clusterInfo.setHealthChecker(clusterMetadata.getHealthChecker());
    99	            clusterInfo.setMetadata(clusterMetadata.getExtendData());
   100	            clusterInfo.setUseInstancePortForCheck(clusterMetadata.isUseInstancePortForCheck());
   101	            clusterInfo.setHealthyCheckPort(clusterMetadata.getHealthyCheckPort());
   102	            clusters.put(each, clusterInfo);
   103	        }
   104	        result.setClusterMap(clusters);
   105	        return result;
   106	    }
   107	    
   108	    @Override
   109	    public List<? extends Instance> listInstances(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName,
   110	            String clusterName) throws NacosException {
   111	        Service service = Service.newService(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName);
   112	        if (!ServiceManager.getInstance().containSingleton(service)) {
   113	            throw new NacosException(NacosException.NOT_FOUND,
   114	                    String.format("service %s@@%s is not found!", groupName, serviceName));
   115	        }
   116	        if (!serviceStorage.getClusters(service).contains(clusterName)) {
   117	            throw new NacosException(NacosException.NOT_FOUND, "cluster " + clusterName + " is not found!");
   118	        }
   119	        ServiceInfo serviceInfo = serviceStorage.getData(service);
   120	        ServiceInfo result = ServiceUtil.selectInstances(serviceInfo, clusterName);
   121	        return result.getHosts();
   122	    }
   123	    
   124	    @Override
   125	    public List<? extends Instance> listAllInstances(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName) {
   126	        Service service = Service.newService(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName);
   127	        if (!ServiceManager.getInstance().containSingleton(service)) {
   128	            return Collections.EMPTY_LIST;
   129	        }
   130	        
   131	        ServiceInfo serviceInfo = serviceStorage.getData(service);
   132	        
   133	        return serviceInfo.getHosts();
   134	    }
   135	    
   136	    @Override
   137	    public Object pageListService(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName, int pageNo, int pageSize,
   138	            String instancePattern, boolean ignoreEmptyService) throws NacosException {
   139	        ObjectNode result = JacksonUtils.createEmptyJsonNode();
   140	        List<ServiceView> serviceViews = new LinkedList<>();
   141	        Collection<Service> services = patternServices(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName);
   142	        if (ignoreEmptyService) {
   143	            services = services.stream().filter(each -> 0 != serviceStorage.getData(each).ipCount())
   144	                    .collect(Collectors.toList());
   145	        }
   146	        result.put(FieldsConstants.COUNT, services.size());
   147	        services = doPage(services, pageNo - 1, pageSize);
   148	        for (Service each : services) {
   149	            ServiceMetadata serviceMetadata = metadataManager.getServiceMetadata(each).orElseGet(ServiceMetadata::new);
   150	            ServiceView serviceView = new ServiceView();
   151	            serviceView.setName(each.getName());
   152	            serviceView.setGroupName(each.getGroup());
   153	            serviceView.setClusterCount(serviceStorage.getClusters(each).size());
   154	            serviceView.setIpCount(serviceStorage.getData(each).ipCount());
   155	            serviceView.setHealthyInstanceCount(countHealthyInstance(serviceStorage.getData(each)));
   156	            serviceView.setTriggerFlag(isProtectThreshold(serviceView, serviceMetadata) ? "true" : "false");
   157	            serviceViews.add(serviceView);
   158	        }
   159	        result.set(FieldsConstants.SERVICE_LIST, JacksonUtils.transferToJsonNode(serviceViews));
   160	        return result;
   161	    }
   162	    
   163	    @Override
   164	    public Page<ServiceView> listService(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName, int pageNo,
   165	            int pageSize, boolean ignoreEmptyService) throws NacosException {
   166	        Page<ServiceView> serviceViews = new Page<>();
   167	        Collection<Service> services = patternServices(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName);
   168	        if (ignoreEmptyService) {
   169	            services = services.stream().filter(each -> 0 != serviceStorage.getData(each).ipCount()).toList();
   170	        }
   171	        Page<Service> page = PageUtil.subPage(services.stream().toList(), pageNo, pageSize);
   172	        serviceViews.setTotalCount(page.getTotalCount());
   173	        serviceViews.setPageNumber(page.getPageNumber());
   174	        serviceViews.setPagesAvailable(page.getPagesAvailable());
   175	        for (Service each : page.getPageItems()) {
   176	            ServiceMetadata serviceMetadata = metadataManager.getServiceMetadata(each).orElseGet(ServiceMetadata::new);
   177	            ServiceView serviceView = new ServiceView();
   178	            serviceView.setName(each.getName());
   179	            serviceView.setGroupName(each.getGroup());
   180	            serviceView.setClusterCount(serviceStorage.getClusters(each).size());
   181	            serviceView.setIpCount(serviceStorage.getData(each).ipCount());
   182	            serviceView.setHealthyInstanceCount(countHealthyInstance(serviceStorage.getData(each)));
   183	            serviceView.setTriggerFlag(isProtectThreshold(serviceView, serviceMetadata) ? "true" : "false");
   184	            serviceViews.getPageItems().add(serviceView);
   185	        }
   186	        return serviceViews;
   187	    }
   188	    
   189	    private int countHealthyInstance(ServiceInfo data) {
   190	        int result = 0;
   191	        for (Instance each : data.getHosts()) {
   192	            if (each.isHealthy()) {
   193	                result++;
   194	            }
   195	        }
   196	        return result;
   197	    }
   198	    
   199	    private boolean isProtectThreshold(ServiceView serviceView, ServiceMetadata metadata) {
   200	        return (serviceView.getHealthyInstanceCount() * 1.0 / serviceView.getIpCount())
   201	                <= metadata.getProtectThreshold();
   202	    }
   203	    
   204	    @Override
   205	    public Page<ServiceDetailInfo> pageListServiceDetail(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName,
   206	            int pageNo, int pageSize) throws NacosException {
   207	        Collection<Service> services = patternServices(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName);
   208	        Page<Service> servicePage = PageUtil.subPage(services.stream().toList(), pageNo, pageSize);
   209	        Page<ServiceDetailInfo> result = new Page<>();
   210	        result.setPagesAvailable(servicePage.getPagesAvailable());
   211	        result.setPageNumber(servicePage.getPageNumber());
   212	        result.setTotalCount(servicePage.getTotalCount());
   213	        List<ServiceDetailInfo> pagedItem = new LinkedList<>();
   214	        for (Service each : servicePage.getPageItems()) {
   215	            ServiceDetailInfo serviceDetailInfo = new ServiceDetailInfo();
   216	            serviceDetailInfo.setServiceName(each.getName());
   217	            serviceDetailInfo.setGroupName(each.getGroup());
   218	            ServiceMetadata serviceMetadata = metadataManager.getServiceMetadata(each).orElseGet(ServiceMetadata::new);
   219	            serviceDetailInfo.setMetadata(serviceMetadata.getExtendData());
   220	            serviceDetailInfo.setClusterMap(getClusterMap(each));
   221	            pagedItem.add(serviceDetailInfo);
   222	        }
   223	        result.setPageItems(pagedItem);
   224	        return result;
   225	    }
   226	    
   227	    private Map<String, ClusterInfo> getClusterMap(Service service) {
   228	        Map<String, ClusterInfo> result = new HashMap<>(1);
   229	        for (Instance each : serviceStorage.getData(service).getHosts()) {
   230	            if (!result.containsKey(each.getClusterName())) {
   231	                ClusterInfo clusterInfo = new ClusterInfo();
   232	                clusterInfo.setHosts(new LinkedList<>());
   233	                result.put(each.getClusterName(), clusterInfo);
   234	            }
   235	            result.get(each.getClusterName()).getHosts().add(each);
   236	        }
   237	        return result;
   238	    }
   239	    
   240	    private Collection<Service> patternServices(String namespaceId, String group, String serviceName) {
   241	        boolean noFilter = StringUtils.isBlank(serviceName) && StringUtils.isBlank(group);
   242	        if (noFilter) {
   243	            return ServiceManager.getInstance().getSingletons(namespaceId);
   244	        }
   245	        Collection<Service> result = new LinkedList<>();
   246	        StringJoiner regex = new StringJoiner(Constants.SERVICE_INFO_SPLITER);
   247	        regex.add(getRegexString(group));
   248	        regex.add(getRegexString(serviceName));
   249	        String regexString = regex.toString();
   250	        for (Service each : ServiceManager.getInstance().getSingletons(namespaceId)) {
   251	            if (each.getGroupedServiceName().matches(regexString)) {
   252	                result.add(each);
   253	            }
   254	        }
   255	        return result;
   256	    }
   257	    
   258	    private String getRegexString(String target) {
   259	        return StringUtils.isBlank(target) ? Constants.ANY_PATTERN
   260	                : Constants.ANY_PATTERN + target + Constants.ANY_PATTERN;
   261	    }
   262	    
   263	    private Collection<Service> doPage(Collection<Service> services, int pageNo, int pageSize) {
   264	        if (pageNo == 0 && services.size() < pageSize) {
   265	            return services;
   266	        }
   267	        int start = pageNo * pageSize;
   268	        if (start > services.size()) {
   269	            return Collections.emptyList();
   270	        }
   271	        Collection<Service> result = new LinkedList<>();
   272	        int i = 0;
   273	        for (Service each : services) {
   274	            if (i++ < start) {
   275	                continue;
   276	            }
   277	            result.add(each);
   278	            if (result.size() >= pageSize) {
   279	                break;
   280	            }
   281	        }
   282	        return result;
   283	    }
   284	}

    26	import com.alibaba.nacos.core.namespace.filter.NamespaceValidation;
    27	import com.alibaba.nacos.core.paramcheck.ExtractorManager;
    28	import com.alibaba.nacos.core.paramcheck.impl.ServiceQueryRequestParamExtractor;
    29	import com.alibaba.nacos.core.remote.RequestHandler;
    30	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.core.v2.index.ServiceStorage;
    31	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.core.v2.metadata.NamingMetadataManager;
    32	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.core.v2.metadata.ServiceMetadata;
    33	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.core.v2.pojo.Service;
    34	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.utils.NamingRequestUtil;
    35	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.utils.ServiceUtil;
    36	import com.alibaba.nacos.plugin.auth.constant.ActionTypes;
    37	import org.springframework.stereotype.Component;
    38	
    39	/**
    40	 * Nacos query instances request handler.
    41	 *
    42	 * @author xiweng.yy
    43	 */
    44	@Component
    45	public class ServiceQueryRequestHandler extends RequestHandler<ServiceQueryRequest, QueryServiceResponse> {
    46	    
    47	    private final ServiceStorage serviceStorage;
    48	    
    49	    private final NamingMetadataManager metadataManager;
    50	    
    51	    public ServiceQueryRequestHandler(ServiceStorage serviceStorage, NamingMetadataManager metadataManager) {
    52	        this.serviceStorage = serviceStorage;
    53	        this.metadataManager = metadataManager;
    54	    }
    55	    
    56	    @Override
    57	    @NamespaceValidation
    58	    @TpsControl(pointName = "RemoteNamingServiceQuery", name = "RemoteNamingServiceQuery")
    59	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.READ)
    60	    @ExtractorManager.Extractor(rpcExtractor = ServiceQueryRequestParamExtractor.class)
    61	    public QueryServiceResponse handle(ServiceQueryRequest request, RequestMeta meta) throws NacosException {
    62	        String namespaceId = request.getNamespace();
    63	        String groupName = request.getGroupName();
    64	        String serviceName = request.getServiceName();
    65	        Service service = Service.newService(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName);
    66	        String cluster = null == request.getCluster() ? "" : request.getCluster();
    67	        boolean healthyOnly = request.isHealthyOnly();
    68	        ServiceInfo result = serviceStorage.getData(service);
    69	        ServiceMetadata serviceMetadata = metadataManager.getServiceMetadata(service).orElse(null);
    70	        result = ServiceUtil.selectInstancesWithHealthyProtection(result, serviceMetadata, cluster, healthyOnly, true,
    71	                NamingRequestUtil.getSourceIpForGrpcRequest(meta));
    72	        return QueryServiceResponse.buildSuccessResponse(result);
    73	    }
    74	}

    46	/**

    51	public final class ServiceUtil {
    52	    
    53	    private static final int DEFAULT_PORT = 80;
    54	    
    55	    /**
    56	     * TODO removed after console controller and console-ui support use ServiceDetailInfo directly.
    57	     *
    58	     * @param serviceDetailInfo serviceDetailInfo
    59	     * @return old console ui custom result
    60	     */
    61	    public static Object transferToConsoleResult(ServiceDetailInfo serviceDetailInfo) {
    62	        ObjectNode serviceObject = JacksonUtils.createEmptyJsonNode();
    63	        serviceObject.put(FieldsConstants.NAME, serviceDetailInfo.getServiceName());
    64	        serviceObject.put(FieldsConstants.GROUP_NAME, serviceDetailInfo.getGroupName());
    65	        serviceObject.put(FieldsConstants.PROTECT_THRESHOLD, serviceDetailInfo.getProtectThreshold());
    66	        serviceObject.replace(FieldsConstants.SELECTOR,
    67	                JacksonUtils.transferToJsonNode(serviceDetailInfo.getSelector()));
    68	        serviceObject.replace(FieldsConstants.METADATA,
    69	                JacksonUtils.transferToJsonNode(serviceDetailInfo.getMetadata()));
    70	        
    71	        ObjectNode detailView = JacksonUtils.createEmptyJsonNode();
    72	        detailView.replace(FieldsConstants.SERVICE, serviceObject);
    73	        
    74	        List<com.alibaba.nacos.api.naming.pojo.Cluster> clusters = new ArrayList<>();
    75	        String groupedServiceName = NamingUtils.getGroupedName(serviceDetailInfo.getServiceName(),
    76	                serviceDetailInfo.getGroupName());
    77	        for (Map.Entry<String, ClusterInfo> entry : serviceDetailInfo.getClusterMap().entrySet()) {
    78	            com.alibaba.nacos.api.naming.pojo.Cluster clusterView = new Cluster();
    79	            clusterView.setName(entry.getKey());
    80	            clusterView.setHealthChecker(entry.getValue().getHealthChecker());
    81	            clusterView.setMetadata(entry.getValue().getMetadata());
    82	            clusterView.setDefaultPort(DEFAULT_PORT);
    83	            clusterView.setUseIpPort4Check(entry.getValue().isUseInstancePortForCheck());
    84	            clusterView.setDefaultCheckPort(entry.getValue().getHealthyCheckPort());
    85	            clusterView.setServiceName(groupedServiceName);
    86	            clusters.add(clusterView);
    87	        }
    88	        
    89	        detailView.replace(FieldsConstants.CLUSTERS, JacksonUtils.transferToJsonNode(clusters));
    90	        return detailView;
    91	    }
    92	    
    93	    /**
    94	     * Page service name.
    95	     *
    96	     * @param pageNo         page number
    97	     * @param pageSize       size per page
    98	     * @param serviceNameSet service name set
    99	     * @return service name list by paged
   100	     */
   101	    public static List<String> pageServiceName(int pageNo, int pageSize, Collection<String> serviceNameSet) {
   102	        List<String> result = new ArrayList<>(serviceNameSet);
   103	        int start = (pageNo - 1) * pageSize;
   104	        if (start < 0) {
   105	            start = 0;
   106	        }
   107	        if (start >= result.size()) {
   108	            return Collections.emptyList();
   109	        }
   110	        int end = start + pageSize;
   111	        if (end > result.size()) {
   112	            end = result.size();
   113	        }
   114	        for (int i = start; i < end; i++) {
   115	            String serviceName = result.get(i);
   116	            int indexOfSplitter = serviceName.indexOf(Constants.SERVICE_INFO_SPLITER);
   117	            if (indexOfSplitter > 0) {
   118	                serviceName = serviceName.substring(indexOfSplitter + 2);
   119	            }
   120	            result.set(i, serviceName);
   121	        }
   122	        return result.subList(start, end);
   123	    }

   125	    /**
   126	     * Select healthy instance of service info.

   132	        return selectInstances(serviceInfo, true, false);
   133	    }

   141	    public static ServiceInfo selectEnabledInstances(ServiceInfo serviceInfo) {
   142	        return selectInstances(serviceInfo, false, true);
   143	    }

   146	     * Select instance of service info.

   154	    }

   157	     * Select instance of service info.

   160	     * @param healthyOnly whether only select instance which healthy
   161	     * @param enableOnly  whether only select instance which enabled
   162	     * @return new service info
   163	     */
   164	    public static ServiceInfo selectInstances(ServiceInfo serviceInfo, boolean healthyOnly, boolean enableOnly) {
   165	        return selectInstances(serviceInfo, StringUtils.EMPTY, healthyOnly, enableOnly);
   166	    }
   167	    
   168	    /**
   169	     * Select instance of service info.
   170	     *
   171	     * @param serviceInfo original service info
   172	     * @param cluster     cluster of instances
   173	     * @param healthyOnly whether only select instance which healthy
   174	     * @return new service info
   175	     */
   176	    public static ServiceInfo selectInstances(ServiceInfo serviceInfo, String cluster, boolean healthyOnly) {
   177	        return selectInstances(serviceInfo, cluster, healthyOnly, false);
   178	    }
   179	    
   180	    /**
   181	     * Select instance of service info.
   182	     *
   183	     * @param serviceInfo original service info
   184	     * @param cluster     cluster of instances
   185	     * @param healthyOnly whether only select instance which healthy
   186	     * @param enableOnly  whether only select instance which enabled
   187	     * @return new service info
   188	     */
   189	    public static ServiceInfo selectInstances(ServiceInfo serviceInfo, String cluster, boolean healthyOnly,
   190	            boolean enableOnly) {
   191	        return doSelectInstances(serviceInfo, cluster, healthyOnly, enableOnly, null);
   192	    }
   193	    
   194	    /**
   195	     * Select instance of service info with healthy protection.
   196	     *
   197	     * @param serviceInfo     original service info
   198	     * @param serviceMetadata service meta info
   199	     * @param subscriber subscriber
   200	     * @return new service info
   201	     */
   202	    public static ServiceInfo selectInstancesWithHealthyProtection(ServiceInfo serviceInfo, ServiceMetadata serviceMetadata, Subscriber subscriber) {
   203	        return selectInstancesWithHealthyProtection(serviceInfo, serviceMetadata, subscriber.getCluster(), false, false, subscriber.getIp());
   204	    }
   205	
   206	    /**
   207	     * Select instance of service info with healthy protection.
   208	     *
   209	     * @param serviceInfo     original service info
   210	     * @param serviceMetadata service meta info
   211	     * @param healthyOnly     whether only select instance which healthy
   212	     * @param enableOnly      whether only select instance which enabled
   213	     * @param subscriber subscriber
   214	     * @return new service info
   215	     */
   216	    public static ServiceInfo selectInstancesWithHealthyProtection(ServiceInfo serviceInfo,
   217	            ServiceMetadata serviceMetadata, boolean healthyOnly, boolean enableOnly, Subscriber subscriber) {
   218	        return selectInstancesWithHealthyProtection(serviceInfo, serviceMetadata, subscriber.getCluster(), healthyOnly,
   219	                enableOnly, subscriber.getIp());
   220	    }
   221	
   222	    /**
   223	     * Select instance of service info with healthy protection.
   224	     *
   225	     * @param serviceInfo     original service info
   226	     * @param serviceMetadata service meta info
   227	     * @param cluster         cluster of instances
   228	     * @param healthyOnly     whether only select instance which healthy
   229	     * @param enableOnly      whether only select instance which enabled
   230	     * @param subscriberIp subscriber ip address
   231	     * @return new service info
   232	     */
   233	    public static ServiceInfo selectInstancesWithHealthyProtection(ServiceInfo serviceInfo, ServiceMetadata serviceMetadata, String cluster,
   234	            boolean healthyOnly, boolean enableOnly, String subscriberIp) {
   235	        InstancesFilter filter = (filteredResult, allInstances, healthyCount) -> {
   236	            if (serviceMetadata == null) {
   237	                return;
   238	            }
   239	            allInstances = filteredResult.getHosts();
   240	            int originalTotal = allInstances.size();
   241	            // filter ips using selector
   242	            SelectorManager selectorManager = ApplicationUtils.getBean(SelectorManager.class);
   243	            allInstances = selectorManager.select(serviceMetadata.getSelector(), subscriberIp, allInstances);
   244	            filteredResult.setHosts(allInstances);
   245	            
   246	            // will re-compute healthCount
   247	            long newHealthyCount = healthyCount;
   248	            if (originalTotal != allInstances.size()) {
   249	                newHealthyCount = 0L;
   250	                for (com.alibaba.nacos.api.naming.pojo.Instance allInstance : allInstances) {
   251	                    if (allInstance.isHealthy()) {
   252	                        newHealthyCount++;
   253	                    }
   254	                }
   255	            }
   256	            
   257	            float threshold = serviceMetadata.getProtectThreshold();
   258	            if (threshold < 0) {
   259	                threshold = 0F;
   260	            }
   261	            if ((float) newHealthyCount / allInstances.size() <= threshold) {
   262	                Loggers.SRV_LOG.warn("protect threshold reached, return all ips, service: {}", filteredResult.getName());
   263	                filteredResult.setReachProtectionThreshold(true);
   264	                List<com.alibaba.nacos.api.naming.pojo.Instance> filteredInstances = allInstances.stream()
   265	                        .map(i -> {
   266	                            if (!i.isHealthy()) {
   267	                                i = InstanceUtil.deepCopy(i);
   268	                                // set all to `healthy` state to protect
   269	                                i.setHealthy(true);
   270	                            } // else deepcopy is unnecessary
   271	                            return i;
   272	                        })
   273	                        .collect(Collectors.toCollection(LinkedList::new));
   274	                filteredResult.setHosts(filteredInstances);
   275	            }
   276	        };
   277	        return doSelectInstances(serviceInfo, cluster, healthyOnly, enableOnly, filter);
   278	    }
   279	
   280	    /**
   281	     * Select instance of service info.
   282	     *
   283	     * @param serviceInfo original service info
   284	     * @param cluster     cluster of instances
   285	     * @param healthyOnly whether only select instance which healthy
   286	     * @param enableOnly  whether only select instance which enabled
   287	     * @param filter      do some other filter operation
   288	     * @return new service info
   289	     */
   290	    private static ServiceInfo doSelectInstances(ServiceInfo serviceInfo, String cluster,
   291	                                                 boolean healthyOnly, boolean enableOnly,
   292	                                                 InstancesFilter filter) {
   293	        ServiceInfo result = new ServiceInfo();
   294	        result.setName(serviceInfo.getName());
   295	        result.setGroupName(serviceInfo.getGroupName());
   296	        result.setCacheMillis(serviceInfo.getCacheMillis());
   297	        result.setLastRefTime(System.currentTimeMillis());
   298	        result.setClusters(cluster);
   299	        result.setReachProtectionThreshold(false);
   300	        Set<String> clusterSets = com.alibaba.nacos.common.utils.StringUtils.isNotBlank(cluster) ? new HashSet<>(
   301	                Arrays.asList(cluster.split(","))) : new HashSet<>();
   302	        long healthyCount = 0L;
   303	        // The instance list won't be modified almost time.
   304	        List<com.alibaba.nacos.api.naming.pojo.Instance> filteredInstances = new LinkedList<>();
   305	        // The instance list of all filtered by cluster/enabled condition.
   306	        List<com.alibaba.nacos.api.naming.pojo.Instance> allInstances = new LinkedList<>();
   307	        for (com.alibaba.nacos.api.naming.pojo.Instance ip : serviceInfo.getHosts()) {
   308	            if (checkCluster(clusterSets, ip) && checkEnabled(enableOnly, ip)) {
   309	                if (!healthyOnly || ip.isHealthy()) {
   310	                    filteredInstances.add(ip);
   311	                }
   312	                if (ip.isHealthy()) {
   313	                    healthyCount += 1;
   314	                }
   315	                allInstances.add(ip);
   316	            }
   317	        }
   318	        result.setHosts(filteredInstances);
   319	        if (filter != null) {
   320	            filter.doFilter(result, allInstances, healthyCount);
   321	        }
   322	        return result;
   323	    }
   324	    
   325	    private static boolean checkCluster(Set<String> clusterSets, com.alibaba.nacos.api.naming.pojo.Instance instance) {
   326	        if (clusterSets.isEmpty()) {
   327	            return true;
   328	        }
   329	        return clusterSets.contains(instance.getClusterName());
   330	    }
   331	    
   332	    private static boolean checkEnabled(boolean enableOnly, com.alibaba.nacos.api.naming.pojo.Instance instance) {
   333	        return !enableOnly || instance.isEnabled();
   334	    }
   335	
   336	    private interface InstancesFilter {
   337	
   338	        /**
   339	         * Do customized filtering.
   340	         *
   341	         * @param filteredResult result with instances already been filtered cluster/enabled/healthy
   342	         * @param allInstances   all instances filtered by cluster/enabled
   343	         * @param healthyCount   healthy instances count filtered by cluster/enabled
   344	         */
   345	        void doFilter(ServiceInfo filteredResult,
   346	                      List<com.alibaba.nacos.api.naming.pojo.Instance> allInstances,
   347	                      long healthyCount);
   348	
   349	    }
   350	
   351	}

    31	import com.alibaba.nacos.common.trace.event.naming.UpdateInstanceTraceEvent;
    32	import com.alibaba.nacos.common.utils.JacksonUtils;
    33	import com.alibaba.nacos.common.utils.StringUtils;
    34	import com.alibaba.nacos.core.control.TpsControl;
    35	import com.alibaba.nacos.core.paramcheck.ExtractorManager;
    36	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.core.CatalogService;
    37	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.core.InstanceOperatorClientImpl;
    38	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.core.InstancePatchObject;
    39	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.misc.Loggers;
    40	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.misc.SwitchDomain;
    41	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.misc.UtilsAndCommons;
    42	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.model.form.InstanceForm;
    43	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.model.form.InstanceListForm;
    44	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.model.form.InstanceMetadataBatchOperationForm;
    45	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.paramcheck.NamingDefaultHttpParamExtractor;
    46	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.paramcheck.NamingInstanceListHttpParamExtractor;
    47	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.paramcheck.NamingInstanceMetadataBatchHttpParamExtractor;
    48	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.pojo.InstanceOperationInfo;
    49	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.utils.InstanceUtil;
    50	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.utils.NamingRequestUtil;
    51	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.web.CanDistro;
    52	import com.alibaba.nacos.plugin.auth.constant.ActionTypes;
    53	import com.fasterxml.jackson.core.type.TypeReference;
    54	import org.apache.commons.collections.CollectionUtils;
    55	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.DeleteMapping;
    56	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.GetMapping;
    57	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.PostMapping;
    58	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.PutMapping;
    59	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestMapping;
    60	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RestController;
    61	
    62	import java.util.ArrayList;
    63	import java.util.Collections;
    64	import java.util.List;
    65	import java.util.Map;
    66	
    67	import static com.alibaba.nacos.naming.misc.UtilsAndCommons.DEFAULT_CLUSTER_NAME;
    68	
    69	/**
    70	 * Instance controller.
    71	 *
    72	 * @author Nacos
    73	 */
    74	@NacosApi
    75	@RestController
    76	@RequestMapping(UtilsAndCommons.INSTANCE_CONTROLLER_V3_ADMIN_PATH)
    77	@ExtractorManager.Extractor(httpExtractor = NamingDefaultHttpParamExtractor.class)
    78	public class InstanceControllerV3 {
    79	    
    80	    private final SwitchDomain switchDomain;
    81	    
    82	    private final InstanceOperatorClientImpl instanceService;
    83	    
    84	    private final CatalogService catalogService;
    85	    
    86	    public InstanceControllerV3(SwitchDomain switchDomain, InstanceOperatorClientImpl instanceService,
    87	            CatalogService catalogService) {
    88	        this.switchDomain = switchDomain;
    89	        this.instanceService = instanceService;
    90	        this.catalogService = catalogService;
    91	    }
    92	    
    93	    /**
    94	     * Register new instance.
    95	     */
    96	    @CanDistro
    97	    @PostMapping
    98	    @TpsControl(pointName = "NamingInstanceRegister", name = "HttpNamingInstanceRegister")
    99	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.WRITE, apiType = ApiType.ADMIN_API)
   100	    public Result<String> register(InstanceForm instanceForm) throws NacosException {
   101	        // check param
   102	        instanceForm.validate();
   103	        NamingRequestUtil.checkWeight(instanceForm.getWeight());
   104	        // build instance
   105	        Instance instance = InstanceUtil.buildInstance(instanceForm, switchDomain.isDefaultInstanceEphemeral());
   106	        String namespaceId = instanceForm.getNamespaceId();
   107	        String groupName = instanceForm.getGroupName();
   108	        String serviceName = instanceForm.getServiceName();
   109	        instanceService.registerInstance(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName, instance);
   110	        NotifyCenter.publishEvent(
   111	                new RegisterInstanceTraceEvent(System.currentTimeMillis(), NamingRequestUtil.getSourceIp(), false,
   112	                        namespaceId, groupName, serviceName, instance.getIp(), instance.getPort()));
   113	        
   114	        return Result.success("ok");
   115	    }
   116	    
   117	    /**
   118	     * Deregister instances.
   119	     */
   120	    @CanDistro
   121	    @DeleteMapping
   122	    @TpsControl(pointName = "NamingInstanceDeregister", name = "HttpNamingInstanceDeregister")
   123	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.WRITE, apiType = ApiType.ADMIN_API)
   124	    public Result<String> deregister(InstanceForm instanceForm) throws NacosException {
   125	        // check param
   126	        instanceForm.validate();
   127	        // build instance
   128	        Instance instance = InstanceUtil.buildInstance(instanceForm, switchDomain.isDefaultInstanceEphemeral());
   129	        instanceService.removeInstance(instanceForm.getNamespaceId(), instanceForm.getGroupName(),
   130	                instanceForm.getServiceName(), instance);
   131	        NotifyCenter.publishEvent(
   132	                new DeregisterInstanceTraceEvent(System.currentTimeMillis(), NamingRequestUtil.getSourceIp(), false,
   133	                        DeregisterInstanceReason.REQUEST, instanceForm.getNamespaceId(), instanceForm.getGroupName(),
   134	                        instanceForm.getServiceName(), instance.getIp(), instance.getPort()));
   135	        
   136	        return Result.success("ok");
   137	    }
   138	    
   139	    /**
   140	     * Update instance.
   141	     */
   142	    @CanDistro
   143	    @PutMapping
   144	    @TpsControl(pointName = "NamingInstanceUpdate", name = "HttpNamingInstanceUpdate")
   145	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.WRITE, apiType = ApiType.ADMIN_API)
   146	    public Result<String> update(InstanceForm instanceForm) throws NacosException {
   147	        // check param
   148	        instanceForm.validate();
   149	        NamingRequestUtil.checkWeight(instanceForm.getWeight());
   150	        // build instance
   151	        Instance instance = InstanceUtil.buildInstance(instanceForm, switchDomain.isDefaultInstanceEphemeral());
   152	        instanceService.updateInstance(instanceForm.getNamespaceId(), instanceForm.getGroupName(),
   153	                instanceForm.getServiceName(), instance);
   154	        NotifyCenter.publishEvent(
   155	                new UpdateInstanceTraceEvent(System.currentTimeMillis(), NamingRequestUtil.getSourceIp(),
   156	                        instanceForm.getNamespaceId(), instanceForm.getGroupName(), instanceForm.getServiceName(),
   157	                        instance.getIp(), instance.getPort(), instance.getMetadata()));
   158	        
   159	        return Result.success("ok");
   160	    }
   161	    
   162	    /**
   163	     * Batch update instance's metadata. old key exist = update, old key not exist = add.
   164	     */
   165	    @CanDistro
   166	    @PutMapping(value = "/metadata/batch")
   167	    @TpsControl(pointName = "NamingInstanceMetadataUpdate", name = "HttpNamingInstanceMetadataBatchUpdate")
   168	    @ExtractorManager.Extractor(httpExtractor = NamingInstanceMetadataBatchHttpParamExtractor.class)
   169	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.WRITE, apiType = ApiType.ADMIN_API)
   170	    public Result<InstanceMetadataBatchResult> batchUpdateInstanceMetadata(InstanceMetadataBatchOperationForm form)
   171	            throws NacosException {
   172	        form.validate();
   173	        
   174	        List<Instance> targetInstances = parseBatchInstances(form.getInstances());
   175	        Map<String, String> targetMetadata = UtilsAndCommons.parseMetadata(form.getMetadata());
   176	        InstanceOperationInfo instanceOperationInfo = buildOperationInfo(buildCompositeServiceName(form),
   177	                form.getConsistencyType(), targetInstances);
   178	        
   179	        List<String> operatedInstances = instanceService.batchUpdateMetadata(form.getNamespaceId(),
   180	                instanceOperationInfo, targetMetadata);
   181	        ArrayList<String> ipList = new ArrayList<>(operatedInstances);
   182	        
   183	        return Result.success(new InstanceMetadataBatchResult(ipList));
   184	    }
   185	    
   186	    /**
   187	     * Batch delete instance's metadata. old key exist = delete, old key not exist = not operate
   188	     */
   189	    @CanDistro
   190	    @DeleteMapping("/metadata/batch")
   191	    @TpsControl(pointName = "NamingInstanceMetadataUpdate", name = "HttpNamingInstanceMetadataBatchUpdate")
   192	    @ExtractorManager.Extractor(httpExtractor = NamingInstanceMetadataBatchHttpParamExtractor.class)
   193	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.WRITE, apiType = ApiType.ADMIN_API)
   194	    public Result<InstanceMetadataBatchResult> batchDeleteInstanceMetadata(InstanceMetadataBatchOperationForm form)
   195	            throws NacosException {
   196	        form.validate();
   197	        List<Instance> targetInstances = parseBatchInstances(form.getInstances());
   198	        Map<String, String> targetMetadata = UtilsAndCommons.parseMetadata(form.getMetadata());
   199	        InstanceOperationInfo instanceOperationInfo = buildOperationInfo(buildCompositeServiceName(form),
   200	                form.getConsistencyType(), targetInstances);
   201	        List<String> operatedInstances = instanceService.batchDeleteMetadata(form.getNamespaceId(),
   202	                instanceOperationInfo, targetMetadata);
   203	        ArrayList<String> ipList = new ArrayList<>(operatedInstances);
   204	        
   205	        return Result.success(new InstanceMetadataBatchResult(ipList));
   206	    }
   207	    
   208	    private InstanceOperationInfo buildOperationInfo(String serviceName, String consistencyType,
   209	            List<Instance> instances) {
   210	        if (!CollectionUtils.isEmpty(instances)) {
   211	            for (Instance instance : instances) {
   212	                if (StringUtils.isBlank(instance.getClusterName())) {
   213	                    instance.setClusterName(DEFAULT_CLUSTER_NAME);
   214	                }
   215	            }
   216	        }
   217	        return new InstanceOperationInfo(serviceName, consistencyType, instances);
   218	    }
   219	    
   220	    private List<Instance> parseBatchInstances(String instances) {
   221	        try {
   222	            return JacksonUtils.toObj(instances, new TypeReference<List<Instance>>() {
   223	            });
   224	        } catch (Exception e) {
   225	            Loggers.SRV_LOG.warn("UPDATE-METADATA: Param 'instances' is illegal, ignore this operation", e);
   226	        }
   227	        return Collections.emptyList();
   228	    }
   229	    
   230	    /**
   231	     * Partial update instance.
   232	     */
   233	    @CanDistro
   234	    @PutMapping(value = "/partial")
   235	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.WRITE, apiType = ApiType.ADMIN_API)
   236	    public Result<String> partialUpdateInstance(InstanceForm instanceForm) throws Exception {
   237	        instanceForm.validate();
   238	        InstancePatchObject patchObject = new InstancePatchObject(instanceForm.getClusterName(), instanceForm.getIp(),
   239	                instanceForm.getPort());
   240	        String metadata = instanceForm.getMetadata();
   241	        if (StringUtils.isNotBlank(metadata)) {
   242	            patchObject.setMetadata(UtilsAndCommons.parseMetadata(metadata));
   243	        }
   244	        Double weight = instanceForm.getWeight();
   245	        if (weight != null) {
   246	            NamingRequestUtil.checkWeight(weight);
   247	            patchObject.setWeight(weight);
   248	        }
   249	        Boolean enabled = instanceForm.getEnabled();
   250	        if (enabled != null) {
   251	            patchObject.setEnabled(enabled);
   252	        }
   253	        instanceService.patchInstance(instanceForm.getNamespaceId(), instanceForm.getGroupName(),
   254	                instanceForm.getServiceName(), patchObject);
   255	        return Result.success("ok");
   256	    }
   257	    
   258	    /**
   259	     * Get all instance of input service.
   260	     */
   261	    @GetMapping("/list")
   262	    @TpsControl(pointName = "NamingServiceSubscribe", name = "HttpNamingServiceSubscribe")
   263	    @ExtractorManager.Extractor(httpExtractor = NamingInstanceListHttpParamExtractor.class)
   264	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.READ, apiType = ApiType.ADMIN_API)
   265	    public Result<List<? extends Instance>> list(InstanceListForm instanceListForm) throws NacosException {
   266	        instanceListForm.validate();
   267	        List<? extends Instance> instances = catalogService.listInstances(instanceListForm.getNamespaceId(),
   268	                instanceListForm.getGroupName(), instanceListForm.getServiceName(), instanceListForm.getClusterName());
   269	        if (instanceListForm.getHealthyOnly()) {
   270	            instances = instances.stream().filter(Instance::isHealthy).toList();
   271	        }
   272	        return Result.success(instances);
   273	    }
   274	    
   275	    /**
   276	     * Get detail information of specified instance.
   277	     */
   278	    @GetMapping
   279	    @TpsControl(pointName = "NamingInstanceQuery", name = "HttpNamingInstanceQuery")
   280	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.READ, apiType = ApiType.ADMIN_API)
   281	    public Result<Instance> detail(InstanceForm instanceForm) throws NacosException {
   282	        instanceForm.validate();
   283	        String namespaceId = instanceForm.getNamespaceId();
   284	        String clusterName = instanceForm.getClusterName();
   285	        String ip = instanceForm.getIp();
   286	        int port = instanceForm.getPort();
   287	        Instance instance = instanceService.getInstance(namespaceId, instanceForm.getGroupName(),
   288	                instanceForm.getServiceName(), clusterName, ip, port);
   289	        return Result.success(instance);
   290	    }
   291	    
   292	    private String buildCompositeServiceName(InstanceMetadataBatchOperationForm form) {
   293	        return NamingUtils.getGroupedName(form.getServiceName(), form.getGroupName());
   294	    }
   295	    
   296	}

    17	package com.alibaba.nacos.naming.controllers.v3;
    18	
    19	import com.alibaba.nacos.api.annotation.NacosApi;
    20	import com.alibaba.nacos.api.common.ApiType;

    27	import com.alibaba.nacos.auth.annotation.Secured;
    28	import com.alibaba.nacos.common.notify.NotifyCenter;
    29	import com.alibaba.nacos.common.trace.DeregisterInstanceReason;
    30	import com.alibaba.nacos.common.trace.event.naming.DeregisterInstanceTraceEvent;
    31	import com.alibaba.nacos.common.trace.event.naming.RegisterInstanceTraceEvent;
    32	import com.alibaba.nacos.core.control.TpsControl;
    33	import com.alibaba.nacos.core.paramcheck.ExtractorManager;
    34	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.core.InstanceOperator;
    35	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.misc.SwitchDomain;
    36	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.misc.UtilsAndCommons;

    38	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.model.form.InstanceListForm;
    39	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.paramcheck.NamingDefaultHttpParamExtractor;
    40	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.paramcheck.NamingInstanceListHttpParamExtractor;
    41	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.pojo.instance.BeatInfoInstanceBuilder;
    42	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.utils.InstanceUtil;
    43	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.utils.NamingRequestUtil;
    44	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.web.CanDistro;
    45	import com.alibaba.nacos.plugin.auth.constant.ActionTypes;
    46	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.DeleteMapping;
    47	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.GetMapping;
    48	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.PostMapping;
    49	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestMapping;
    50	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestParam;
    51	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RestController;
    52	
    53	import java.util.List;
    54	
    55	/**
    56	 * Nacos naming module client used HTTP Open API controller.
    57	 *
    58	 * <p>
    59	 * This open API is used for some program language which not support gRPC request and want to develop a application used
    60	 * client to register/deregister self to Nacos, or get remote call service instance list from Nacos. So this client used
    61	 * open API only provide specified feature APIs to register instance/deregister instance/get instance list for specified
    62	 * service. Not support subscribe service instances with HTTP, please use gRPC request to subscribe service.
    63	 * </p>
    64	 *
    65	 * @author xiweng.yy
    66	 */
    67	@NacosApi
    68	@RestController
    69	@RequestMapping(UtilsAndCommons.INSTANCE_V3_CLIENT_API_PATH)
    70	@ExtractorManager.Extractor(httpExtractor = NamingDefaultHttpParamExtractor.class)
    71	public class InstanceOpenApiController {
    72	    
    73	    private final InstanceOperator instanceOperator;
    74	    
    75	    private final SwitchDomain switchDomain;
    76	    
    77	    public InstanceOpenApiController(InstanceOperator instanceOperator, SwitchDomain switchDomain) {
    78	        this.instanceOperator = instanceOperator;
    79	        this.switchDomain = switchDomain;
    80	    }
    81	    
    82	    /**
    83	     * Register or heart beat instance to Nacos.
    84	     *
    85	     * @param instanceForm instance form
    86	     * @param heartBeat    whether is heart beat request
    87	     * @return register or heart beat result. If is heartBeat request(heartBeat=true) and instance not found, return
    88	     * code `21003` to indicate caller should register again with heartBeat=false.
    89	     * @throws NacosException register or heart beat with exception.
    90	     */
    91	    @CanDistro
    92	    @PostMapping
    93	    @TpsControl(pointName = "NamingInstanceRegister", name = "HttpNamingInstanceRegister")
    94	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.WRITE, apiType = ApiType.OPEN_API)
    95	    public Result<String> register(InstanceForm instanceForm, @RequestParam(defaultValue = "false") boolean heartBeat)
    96	            throws NacosException {
    97	        // check param
    98	        instanceForm.validate();
    99	        if (heartBeat) {
   100	            if (ResponseCode.OK != doHeartBeat(instanceForm)) {
   101	                return Result.failure(ErrorCode.INSTANCE_NOT_FOUND, null);
   102	            }
   103	        } else {
   104	            doRegisterInstance(instanceForm);
   105	        }
   106	        return Result.success("ok");
   107	    }
   108	    
   109	    /**
   110	     * Deregister instance from Nacos.
   111	     *
   112	     * @param instanceForm instance form
   113	     * @return deregister result, if instance not found, also return remove success.
   114	     * @throws NacosException deregister with exception.
   115	     */
   116	    @CanDistro
   117	    @DeleteMapping
   118	    @TpsControl(pointName = "NamingInstanceDeregister", name = "HttpNamingInstanceDeregister")
   119	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.WRITE, apiType = ApiType.OPEN_API)
   120	    public Result<String> deregister(InstanceForm instanceForm) throws NacosException {
   121	        // check param
   122	        instanceForm.validate();
   123	        Instance instance = InstanceUtil.buildInstance(instanceForm, switchDomain.isDefaultInstanceEphemeral());
   124	        instanceOperator.removeInstance(instanceForm.getNamespaceId(), instanceForm.getGroupName(),
   125	                instanceForm.getServiceName(), instance);
   126	        NotifyCenter.publishEvent(
   127	                new DeregisterInstanceTraceEvent(System.currentTimeMillis(), NamingRequestUtil.getSourceIp(), false,
   128	                        DeregisterInstanceReason.REQUEST, instanceForm.getNamespaceId(), instanceForm.getGroupName(),
   129	                        instanceForm.getServiceName(), instance.getIp(), instance.getPort()));
   130	        return Result.success("ok");
   131	    }
   132	    
   133	    /**
   134	     * Get all instances for specified service.
   135	     *
   136	     * <p>
   137	     * This API will not return `enabled=false` instances, because of this api is used by custom client. instances with
   138	     * `enabled=false` means instance has been offline, so client should not found these service instances.
   139	     * </p>
   140	     *
   141	     * @param instanceForm instance form of subscriber. The ip and port is subscriber info. The service name, group name
   142	     *                     and cluster name is the target service info.
   143	     * @return all instances for specified service without `enabled=false`.
   144	     * @throws Exception any exception during get instances.
   145	     */
   146	    @GetMapping("/list")
   147	    @TpsControl(pointName = "NamingServiceSubscribe", name = "HttpNamingServiceSubscribe")
   148	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.READ, apiType = ApiType.OPEN_API)
   149	    @ExtractorManager.Extractor(httpExtractor = NamingInstanceListHttpParamExtractor.class)
   150	    public Result<List<Instance>> list(InstanceListForm instanceForm) throws Exception {
   151	        // check param
   152	        instanceForm.validate();
   153	        String namespaceId = instanceForm.getNamespaceId();
   154	        String groupName = instanceForm.getGroupName();
   155	        String serviceName = instanceForm.getServiceName();
   156	        ServiceInfo serviceInfo = instanceOperator.listInstance(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName, null,
   157	                instanceForm.getClusterName(), false);
   158	        return Result.success(serviceInfo.getHosts());
   159	    }
   160	    
   161	    private int doHeartBeat(InstanceForm instanceForm) throws NacosException {
   162	        BeatInfoInstanceBuilder builder = BeatInfoInstanceBuilder.newBuilder();
   163	        return instanceOperator.handleBeat(instanceForm.getNamespaceId(), instanceForm.getGroupName(),
   164	                instanceForm.getServiceName(), instanceForm.getIp(), instanceForm.getPort(),
   165	                instanceForm.getClusterName(), null, builder);
   166	    }
   167	    
   168	    private void doRegisterInstance(InstanceForm instanceForm) throws NacosException {
   169	        NamingRequestUtil.checkWeight(instanceForm.getWeight());
   170	        Instance instance = InstanceUtil.buildInstance(instanceForm, switchDomain.isDefaultInstanceEphemeral());
   171	        String namespaceId = instanceForm.getNamespaceId();
   172	        String groupName = instanceForm.getGroupName();
   173	        String serviceName = instanceForm.getServiceName();
   174	        instanceOperator.registerInstance(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName, instance);
   175	        NotifyCenter.publishEvent(
   176	                new RegisterInstanceTraceEvent(System.currentTimeMillis(), NamingRequestUtil.getSourceIp(), false,
   177	                        namespaceId, groupName, serviceName, instance.getIp(), instance.getPort()));
   178	    }
   179	}

    20	import com.alibaba.nacos.api.annotation.NacosApi;
    21	import com.alibaba.nacos.api.common.ApiType;
    22	import com.alibaba.nacos.api.exception.NacosException;

    25	import com.alibaba.nacos.api.model.v2.ErrorCode;
    26	import com.alibaba.nacos.api.model.v2.Result;
    27	import com.alibaba.nacos.api.naming.pojo.Instance;
    28	import com.alibaba.nacos.api.naming.pojo.builder.InstanceBuilder;
    29	import com.alibaba.nacos.api.naming.utils.NamingUtils;
    30	import com.alibaba.nacos.auth.annotation.Secured;
    31	import com.alibaba.nacos.console.proxy.naming.InstanceProxy;
    32	import com.alibaba.nacos.core.control.TpsControl;
    33	import com.alibaba.nacos.core.model.form.PageForm;
    34	import com.alibaba.nacos.core.paramcheck.ExtractorManager;
    35	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.misc.UtilsAndCommons;
    36	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.model.form.InstanceForm;
    37	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.model.form.InstanceListForm;
    38	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.paramcheck.NamingDefaultHttpParamExtractor;
    39	import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.web.CanDistro;
    40	import com.alibaba.nacos.plugin.auth.constant.ActionTypes;
    41	import org.springframework.http.HttpStatus;
    42	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.PutMapping;
    43	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RequestMapping;
    44	import org.springframework.web.bind.annotation.RestController;
    45	
    46	/**
    47	 * Controller for handling HTTP requests related to instance operations.
    48	 *
    49	 * @author zhangyukun on:2024/8/16
    50	 */
    51	@NacosApi
    52	@RestController
    53	@RequestMapping("/v3/console/ns/instance")
    54	@ExtractorManager.Extractor(httpExtractor = NamingDefaultHttpParamExtractor.class)
    55	public class ConsoleInstanceController {
    56	    
    57	    private final InstanceProxy instanceProxy;
    58	    
    59	    /**
    60	     * Constructs a new ConsoleInstanceController with the provided InstanceProxy.
    61	     *
    62	     * @param instanceProxy the proxy used for handling instance-related operations
    63	     */
    64	    public ConsoleInstanceController(InstanceProxy instanceProxy) {
    65	        this.instanceProxy = instanceProxy;
    66	    }
    67	    
    68	    /**
    69	     * List instances of special service.
    70	     *
    71	     * @param instanceForm instance list form
    72	     * @param pageForm     Page form
    73	     * @return instances information
    74	     */
    75	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.READ, apiType = ApiType.CONSOLE_API)
    76	    @RequestMapping("/list")
    77	    public Result<Page<? extends Instance>> getInstanceList(InstanceListForm instanceForm, PageForm pageForm)
    78	            throws NacosException {
    79	        instanceForm.validate();
    80	        pageForm.validate();
    81	        Page<? extends Instance> instancePage = instanceProxy.listInstances(instanceForm.getNamespaceId(),
    82	                instanceForm.getServiceName(), instanceForm.getGroupName(), instanceForm.getClusterName(),
    83	                pageForm.getPageNo(), pageForm.getPageSize());
    84	        return Result.success(instancePage);
    85	    }
    86	    
    87	    /**
    88	     * Update instance.
    89	     */
    90	    @CanDistro
    91	    @PutMapping
    92	    @TpsControl(pointName = "NamingInstanceUpdate", name = "HttpNamingInstanceUpdate")
    93	    @Secured(action = ActionTypes.WRITE, apiType = ApiType.CONSOLE_API)
    94	    public Result<String> updateInstance(InstanceForm instanceForm) throws NacosException {
    95	        // check param
    96	        instanceForm.validate();
    97	        checkWeight(instanceForm.getWeight());
    98	        // build instance
    99	        Instance instance = buildInstance(instanceForm);
   100	        instanceProxy.updateInstance(instanceForm, instance);
   101	        return Result.success("ok");
   102	    }
   103	    
   104	    private void checkWeight(Double weight) throws NacosException {
   105	        if (weight > com.alibaba.nacos.naming.constants.Constants.MAX_WEIGHT_VALUE
   106	                || weight < com.alibaba.nacos.naming.constants.Constants.MIN_WEIGHT_VALUE) {
   107	            throw new NacosApiException(HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST.value(), ErrorCode.WEIGHT_ERROR,
   108	                    "instance format invalid: The weights range from "
   109	                            + com.alibaba.nacos.naming.constants.Constants.MIN_WEIGHT_VALUE + " to "
   110	                            + com.alibaba.nacos.naming.constants.Constants.MAX_WEIGHT_VALUE);
   111	        }
   112	    }
   113	    
   114	    private Instance buildInstance(InstanceForm instanceForm) throws NacosException {
   115	        Instance instance = InstanceBuilder.newBuilder().setServiceName(buildCompositeServiceName(instanceForm))
   116	                .setIp(instanceForm.getIp()).setClusterName(instanceForm.getClusterName())
   117	                .setPort(instanceForm.getPort()).setHealthy(instanceForm.getHealthy())
   118	                .setWeight(instanceForm.getWeight()).setEnabled(instanceForm.getEnabled())
   119	                .setMetadata(UtilsAndCommons.parseMetadata(instanceForm.getMetadata()))
   120	                .setEphemeral(instanceForm.getEphemeral()).build();
   121	        if (instanceForm.getEphemeral() == null) {
   122	            // register instance by console default is persistent instance.
   123	            instance.setEphemeral(false);
   124	        }
   125	        return instance;
   126	    }
   127	    
   128	    private String buildCompositeServiceName(InstanceForm instanceForm) {
   129	        return NamingUtils.getGroupedName(instanceForm.getServiceName(), instanceForm.getGroupName());
   130	    }
   131	    
   132	}

    25	import org.springframework.stereotype.Service;
    26	
    27	/**
    28	 * Proxy class for handling instance-related operations.
    29	 *
    30	 * @author zhangyukun
    31	 */
    32	@Service
    33	public class InstanceProxy {
    34	    
    35	    private final InstanceHandler instanceHandler;
    36	    
    37	    /**
    38	     * Constructs a new InstanceProxy with the given InstanceInnerHandler and ConsoleConfig.
    39	     *
    40	     * @param instanceHandler the default implementation of InstanceHandler
    41	     */
    42	    public InstanceProxy(InstanceHandler instanceHandler) {
    43	        this.instanceHandler = instanceHandler;
    44	    }
    45	    
    46	    /**
    47	     * Retrieve a list of instances for a specific service and returns as an ObjectNode.
    48	     *
    49	     * @param namespaceId             the namespace ID
    50	     * @param serviceNameWithoutGroup the service name without group
    51	     * @param groupName               the group name
    52	     * @param clusterName             the cluster name
    53	     * @param page                    the page number
    54	     * @param pageSize                the size of the page
    55	     * @return the page object of {@link Instance}
    56	     * @throws IllegalArgumentException if the deployment type is invalid
    57	     * @throws NacosException           if the list operation fails
    58	     */
    59	    public Page<? extends Instance> listInstances(String namespaceId, String serviceNameWithoutGroup, String groupName,
    60	            String clusterName, int page, int pageSize) throws NacosException {
    61	        return instanceHandler.listInstances(namespaceId, serviceNameWithoutGroup, groupName, clusterName, page,
    62	                pageSize);
    63	    }
    64	    
    65	    /**
    66	     * Updates an instance.
    67	     *
    68	     * @param instanceForm the form containing instance data
    69	     * @param instance     the instance to update
    70	     * @throws NacosException           if the update operation fails
    71	     * @throws IllegalArgumentException if the deployment type is invalid
    72	     */
    73	    public void updateInstance(InstanceForm instanceForm, Instance instance) throws NacosException {
    74	        instanceHandler.updateInstance(instanceForm, instance);
    75	    }
    76	}

2026-05-30 05:42:32,699 - INFO - swea-agent-alibaba__nacos-14778 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now let me understand the issue more clearly. The problem is:

1. **gRPC path**: `ServiceQueryRequestHandler.handle()` - when cluster is null, it sets it to `""` (empty string), then calls `ServiceUtil.selectInstances` which creates an empty `Set` for `clusterSets` (because `StringUtils.isNotBlank("")` is false), and `checkCluster` returns `true` for all instances because `clusterSets.isEmpty()`.

2. **v3 HTTP path**: `InstanceListForm.fillDefaultValue()` - when `clusterName` is blank, it fills it with `"DEFAULT"`, then `CatalogServiceV2Impl.listInstances()` checks if `serviceStorage.getClusters(service).contains("DEFAULT")` - if the cluster name is not "DEFAULT" (e.g., it's something else), it throws `NacosException NOT_FOUND`.

The fix should be in `CatalogServiceV2Impl.listInstances()` to handle the case when `clusterName` is blank/null/empty by falling back to `listAllInstances` logic (i.e., not filtering by cluster).

But wait, there's also the approach of fixing `InstanceListForm.fillDefaultValue()` to not fill default cluster name. Let me think about which approach is better.

Looking at the PR description again:
> 修复方式是 InstanceListForm.fillDefaultValue() 不应该对 clusterName 做默认填充，或者 listInstances 里 clusterName 为空时走 listAllInstances 的逻辑。

Both approaches are suggested. Let me think about which one is more consistent with the gRPC path.

In gRPC: `cluster = null == request.getCluster() ? "" : request.getCluster()` — empty string means "all clusters".

In `ServiceUtil.doSelectInstances`: `clusterSets = StringUtils.isNotBlank("") ? ... : new HashSet<>()` — empty set means all pass.

So the gRPC approach is: empty/blank cluster = match all instances.

For the v3 HTTP path, the fix should make it consistent. The simplest fix would be in `CatalogServiceV2Impl.listInstances()`: if `clusterName` is blank, return all instances (similar to `listAllInstances`). But `listAllInstances` doesn't throw `NOT_FOUND` when service doesn't exist, whereas `listInstances` does. Let me check...

Actually, looking more closely at the `listInstances` method:

```java
public List<? extends Instance> listInstances(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName,
        String clusterName) throws NacosException {
    Service service = Service.newService(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName);
    if (!ServiceManager.getInstance().containSingleton(service)) {
        throw new NacosException(NacosException.NOT_FOUND, ...);
    }
    if (!serviceStorage.getClusters(service).contains(clusterName)) {
        throw new NacosException(NacosException.NOT_FOUND, "cluster " + clusterName + " is not found!");
    }
    ServiceInfo serviceInfo = serviceStorage.getData(service);
    ServiceInfo result = ServiceUtil.selectInstances(serviceInfo, clusterName);
    return result.getHosts();
}
```

And `listAllInstances`:
```java
public List<? extends Instance> listAllInstances(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName) {
    Service service = Service.newService(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName);
    if (!ServiceManager.getInstance().containSingleton(service)) {
        return Collections.EMPTY_LIST;
    }
    ServiceInfo serviceInfo = serviceStorage.getData(service);
    return serviceInfo.getHosts();
}
```

The key difference: `listAllInstances` returns empty list if service not found, while `listInstances` throws an exception. 

Now, the approach I think is best: modify `CatalogServiceV2Impl.listInstances()` to handle blank `clusterName` by not doing the cluster check and passing empty string to `ServiceUtil.selectInstances` (which handles empty string correctly). 

But wait, let me also check the callers. The `InstanceControllerV3.list()` calls `catalogService.listInstances(...)`. The `InstanceOpenApiController.list()` calls `instanceOperator.listInstance(...)`.

Let me check the `InstanceOperator` interface:

    71	@org.springframework.stereotype.Service
    72	public class InstanceOperatorClientImpl implements InstanceOperator {
    73	    
    74	    private final ClientManager clientManager;
    75	    
    76	    private final ClientOperationService clientOperationService;
    77

    79

    83

    85	
    86	    public InstanceOperatorClientImpl(ClientManagerDelegate clientManager,
    87	            ClientOperationServiceProxy clientOperationService, ServiceStorage serviceStorage,
    88	            NamingMetadataOperateService metadataOperateService, NamingMetadataManager metadataManager,
    89	            SwitchDomain switchDomain) {
    90	        this.clientManager = clientManager;
    91	        this.clientOperationService = clientOperationService;
    92	        this.serviceStorage = serviceStorage;
    93	        this.metadataOperateService = metadataOperateService;
    94	        this.metadataManager = metadataManager;
    95	        this.switchDomain = switchDomain;
    96	    }

    98	    /**
    99	     * This method creates {@code IpPortBasedClient} if it doesn't exist.
   100	     */
   101	    @Override
   102	    public void registerInstance(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName, Instance instance)
   103	            throws NacosException {
   104	        NamingUtils.checkInstanceIsLegal(instance);
   105	        boolean ephemeral = instance.isEphemeral();
   106	        String clientId = IpPortBasedClient.getClientId(instance.toInetAddr(), ephemeral);
   107	        createIpPortClientIfAbsent(clientId);
   108	        Service service = Service.newService(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName, ephemeral);
   109	        clientOperationService.registerInstance(service, instance, clientId);
   110	    }
   111	    
   112	    @Override
   113	    public void removeInstance(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName, Instance instance) {
   114	        boolean ephemeral = instance.isEphemeral();
   115	        String clientId = IpPortBasedClient.getClientId(instance.toInetAddr(), ephemeral);
   116	        if (!clientManager.contains(clientId)) {
   117	            Loggers.SRV_LOG.warn("remove instance from non-exist client: {}", clientId);
   118	            return;
   119	        }
   120	        Service service = Service.newService(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName, ephemeral);
   121	        clientOperationService.deregisterInstance(service, instance, clientId);
   122	    }
   123	    
   124	    @Override
   125	    public void updateInstance(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName, Instance instance)
   126	            throws NacosException {
   127	        NamingUtils.checkInstanceIsLegal(instance);
   128	        
   129	        Service service = Service.newService(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName, instance.isEphemeral());
   130	        if (!ServiceManager.getInstance().containSingleton(service)) {
   131	            throw new NacosApiException(NacosException.INVALID_PARAM, ErrorCode.INSTANCE_ERROR,
   132	                    "service not found, namespace: " + namespaceId + ", service: " + service);
   133	        }
   134	        String metadataId = InstancePublishInfo.genMetadataId(instance.getIp(), instance.getPort(),
   135	                instance.getClusterName());
   136	        metadataOperateService.updateInstanceMetadata(service, metadataId, buildMetadata(instance));
   137	        NotifyCenter.publishEvent(new InfoChangeEvent.InstanceInfoChangeEvent(service, instance));
   138	    }
   139	    
   140	    private InstanceMetadata buildMetadata(Instance instance) {
   141	        InstanceMetadata result = new InstanceMetadata();
   142	        result.setEnabled(instance.isEnabled());
   143	        result.setWeight(instance.getWeight());
   144	        result.getExtendData().putAll(filterNullValue(instance.getMetadata()));
   145	        return result;
   146	    }
   147	    
   148	    private Map<String, String> filterNullValue(Map<String, String> metadata) {
   149	        return metadata.entrySet().stream().filter(entry -> entry.getValue() != null)
   150	                .collect(Collectors.toMap(Map.Entry::getKey, Map.Entry::getValue));
   151	    }
   152	    
   153	    @Override
   154	    public void patchInstance(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName, InstancePatchObject patchObject)
   155	            throws NacosException {
   156	        Service service = Service.newService(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName, true);
   157	        Instance instance = getInstance0(service, patchObject.getCluster(), patchObject.getIp(), patchObject.getPort());
   158	        String metadataId = InstancePublishInfo.genMetadataId(instance.getIp(), instance.getPort(),
   159	                instance.getClusterName());
   160	        Optional<InstanceMetadata> instanceMetadata = metadataManager.getInstanceMetadata(service, metadataId);
   161	        InstanceMetadata newMetadata = instanceMetadata.map(this::cloneMetadata).orElseGet(InstanceMetadata::new);
   162	        mergeMetadata(newMetadata, patchObject);
   163	        metadataOperateService.updateInstanceMetadata(service, metadataId, newMetadata);
   164	    }
   165	    
   166	    private InstanceMetadata cloneMetadata(InstanceMetadata instanceMetadata) {
   167	        InstanceMetadata result = new InstanceMetadata();
   168	        result.setExtendData(new HashMap<>(instanceMetadata.getExtendData()));
   169	        result.setWeight(instanceMetadata.getWeight());
   170	        result.setEnabled(instanceMetadata.isEnabled());
   171	        return result;
   172	    }
   173	    
   174	    private void mergeMetadata(InstanceMetadata newMetadata, InstancePatchObject patchObject) {
   175	        if (null != patchObject.getMetadata()) {
   176	            newMetadata.setExtendData(new HashMap<>(patchObject.getMetadata()));
   177	        }
   178	        if (null != patchObject.getEnabled()) {
   179	            newMetadata.setEnabled(patchObject.getEnabled());
   180	        }
   181	        if (null != patchObject.getWeight()) {
   182	            newMetadata.setWeight(patchObject.getWeight());
   183	        }
   184	    }
   185	    
   186	    @Override
   187	    public ServiceInfo listInstance(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName, Subscriber subscriber,
   188	            String cluster, boolean healthOnly) {
   189	        Service service = Service.newService(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName, true);
   190	        // For adapt 1.X subscribe logic

   192	            Loggers.SRV_LOG.warn("[DEPRECATED] UDP push has been removed in Nacos 3.2.0. "

   194	                    + "Please upgrade to Nacos 2.x client with gRPC support. Subscriber: {}",
   195	                    subscriber.getAgent(), subscriber.getAddrStr());
   196	            String clientId = IpPortBasedClient.getClientId(subscriber.getAddrStr(), true);
   197	            createIpPortClientIfAbsent(clientId);
   198	            clientOperationService.subscribeService(service, subscriber, clientId);
   199	        }
   200	        ServiceInfo serviceInfo = serviceStorage.getData(service);

   262	    @Override
   263	    public long getHeartBeatInterval(String namespaceId, String serviceName, String ip, int port, String cluster) {
   264	        Service service = getService(namespaceId, serviceName, true);
   265	        String metadataId = InstancePublishInfo.genMetadataId(ip, port, cluster);
   266	        Optional<InstanceMetadata> metadata = metadataManager.getInstanceMetadata(service, metadataId);
   267	        if (metadata.isPresent() && metadata.get().getExtendData()
   268	                .containsKey(PreservedMetadataKeys.HEART_BEAT_INTERVAL)) {
   269	            return ConvertUtils.toLong(metadata.get().getExtendData().get(PreservedMetadataKeys.HEART_BEAT_INTERVAL));
   270	        }
   271	        String clientId = IpPortBasedClient.getClientId(ip + InternetAddressUtil.IP_PORT_SPLITER + port, true);
   272	        Client client = clientManager.getClient(clientId);
   273	        InstancePublishInfo instance = null != client ? client.getInstancePublishInfo(service) : null;
   274	        if (null != instance && instance.getExtendDatum().containsKey(PreservedMetadataKeys.HEART_BEAT_INTERVAL)) {
   275	            return ConvertUtils.toLong(instance.getExtendDatum().get(PreservedMetadataKeys.HEART_BEAT_INTERVAL));
   276	        }
   277	        return switchDomain.getClientBeatInterval();
   278	    }
