   286	    @Override
   287	    public List<String> batchUpdateMetadata(String namespaceId, InstanceOperationInfo instanceOperationInfo,
   288	            Map<String, String> metadata) throws NacosException {
   289	        boolean isEphemeral = !UtilsAndCommons.PERSIST.equals(instanceOperationInfo.getConsistencyType());
   290	        String serviceName = instanceOperationInfo.getServiceName();
   291	        Service service = getService(namespaceId, serviceName, isEphemeral);
   292	        List<String> result = new LinkedList<>();
   293	        List<Instance> needUpdateInstance = findBatchUpdateInstance(instanceOperationInfo, service);
   294	        for (Instance each : needUpdateInstance) {
   295	            String metadataId = InstancePublishInfo.genMetadataId(each.getIp(), each.getPort(), each.getClusterName());
   296	            Optional<InstanceMetadata> instanceMetadata = metadataManager.getInstanceMetadata(service, metadataId);
   297	            InstanceMetadata newMetadata = instanceMetadata.map(this::cloneMetadata).orElseGet(InstanceMetadata::new);
   298	            newMetadata.getExtendData().putAll(metadata);
   299	            metadataOperateService.updateInstanceMetadata(service, metadataId, newMetadata);
   300	            result.add(each.toInetAddr() + ":" + UtilsAndCommons.LOCALHOST_SITE + ":" + each.getClusterName() + ":" + (
   301	                    each.isEphemeral() ? UtilsAndCommons.EPHEMERAL : UtilsAndCommons.PERSIST));
   302	        }
   303	        return result;
   304	    }
   305	    
   306	    @Override
   307	    public List<String> batchDeleteMetadata(String namespaceId, InstanceOperationInfo instanceOperationInfo,
   308	            Map<String, String> metadata) throws NacosException {
   309	        boolean isEphemeral = !UtilsAndCommons.PERSIST.equals(instanceOperationInfo.getConsistencyType());
   310	        String serviceName = instanceOperationInfo.getServiceName();
   311	        Service service = getService(namespaceId, serviceName, isEphemeral);
   312	        List<String> result = new LinkedList<>();
   313	        List<Instance> needUpdateInstance = findBatchUpdateInstance(instanceOperationInfo, service);
   314	        for (Instance each : needUpdateInstance) {
   315	            String metadataId = InstancePublishInfo.genMetadataId(each.getIp(), each.getPort(), each.getClusterName());
   316	            Optional<InstanceMetadata> instanceMetadata = metadataManager.getInstanceMetadata(service, metadataId);
   317	            InstanceMetadata newMetadata = instanceMetadata.map(this::cloneMetadata).orElseGet(InstanceMetadata::new);
   318	            metadata.keySet().forEach(key -> newMetadata.getExtendData().remove(key));
   319	            metadataOperateService.updateInstanceMetadata(service, metadataId, newMetadata);
   320	            result.add(each.toInetAddr() + ":" + UtilsAndCommons.LOCALHOST_SITE + ":" + each.getClusterName() + ":" + (
   321	                    each.isEphemeral() ? UtilsAndCommons.EPHEMERAL : UtilsAndCommons.PERSIST));
   322	        }
   323	        return result;
   324	    }
   325	    
   326	    private List<Instance> findBatchUpdateInstance(InstanceOperationInfo instanceOperationInfo, Service service) {
   327	        if (null == instanceOperationInfo.getInstances() || instanceOperationInfo.getInstances().isEmpty()) {
   328	            return serviceStorage.getData(service).getHosts();
   329	        }
   330	        List<Instance> result = new LinkedList<>();
   331	        for (Instance each : instanceOperationInfo.getInstances()) {
   332	            try {
   333	                getInstance0(service, each.getClusterName(), each.getIp(), each.getPort());
   334	                result.add(each);
   335	            } catch (NacosException ignored) {
   336	            }
   337	        }
   338	        return result;
   339	    }
   340	    
   341	    private void createIpPortClientIfAbsent(String clientId) {
   342	        if (!clientManager.contains(clientId)) {
   343	            ClientAttributes clientAttributes = ClientAttributesFilter.getCurrentClientAttributes()
   344	                    .orElse(new ClientAttributes());
   345	            clientManager.clientConnected(clientId, clientAttributes);
   346	        }
   347	    }

   349	    private Service getService(String namespaceId, String serviceName, boolean ephemeral) {
   350	        String groupName = NamingUtils.getGroupName(serviceName);
   351	        String serviceNameNoGrouped = NamingUtils.getServiceName(serviceName);
   352	        return Service.newService(namespaceId, groupName, serviceNameNoGrouped, ephemeral);
   353	    }

   224	                return each;
   225	            }

2026-05-30 05:43:16,098 - INFO - swea-agent-alibaba__nacos-14778 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I have a thorough understanding of the issue. Let me summarize:

**The Problem:**
- `InstanceListForm.fillDefaultValue()` sets blank `clusterName` to `"DEFAULT"` (line 71-72).
- `CatalogServiceV2Impl.listInstances()` does an exact cluster match: `serviceStorage.getClusters(service).contains(clusterName)` (line 116). If the cluster is "DEFAULT" but the actual cluster in the service is something else (e.g., "cluster-hba"), it throws `NOT_FOUND`.
- The gRPC path uses `ServiceUtil.doSelectInstances()` which treats empty string as "match all".

**The Fix:**
The best approach is to modify `CatalogServiceV2Impl.listInstances()` to handle blank `clusterName` by treating it as "all clusters" — matching the gRPC behavior. But we also need to fix `InstanceListForm.fillDefaultValue()` to not fill "DEFAULT" into clusterName.

Actually, looking more carefully at the PR description:
> 修复方式是 InstanceListForm.fillDefaultValue() 不应该对 clusterName 做默认填充，或者 listInstances 里 clusterName 为空时走 listAllInstances 的逻辑。

The two approaches are:
1. Don't fill default value for `clusterName` in `InstanceListForm.fillDefaultValue()`
2. In `listInstances`, when `clusterName` is empty, use `listAllInstances` logic

I think the best fix is approach 1 (remove the default filling for clusterName) combined with modifying `CatalogServiceV2Impl.listInstances()` to handle empty/blank clusterName properly by treating it like "all clusters" (similar to gRPC behavior). 

But wait, if we just remove the default filling of `clusterName` in `fillDefaultValue()`, then `clusterName` will be `null` when not provided. Let me trace what happens then:

- `InstanceControllerV3.list()` calls `catalogService.listInstances(..., instanceListForm.getClusterName())` which would pass `null`.
- `CatalogServiceV2Impl.listInstances()` gets `null` clusterName, then line 116: `serviceStorage.getClusters(service).contains(null)` — this would likely return false and throw an exception.

So we need to fix both: either `CatalogServiceV2Impl.listInstances()` to handle null/blank, or `InstanceListForm.fillDefaultValue()` to not fill clusterName and also change the callers.

The cleanest approach from the PR description seems to be: modify `CatalogServiceV2Impl.listInstances()` to handle blank clusterName by not doing the cluster check and passing empty string to `ServiceUtil.selectInstances` (which already handles empty string correctly).

2026-05-30 05:43:34,855 - INFO - swea-agent-alibaba__nacos-14778 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I have a clear view. The constant `DEFAULT_CLUSTER_NAME = "DEFAULT"` is in both `Constants` and `UtilsAndCommons`.

Now, let me think about the right fix:

The PR description says:
> 修复方式是 InstanceListForm.fillDefaultValue() 不应该对 clusterName 做默认填充，或者 listInstances 里 clusterName 为空时走 listAllInstances 的逻辑。

I think the best approach is:
1. **Remove the default filling of `clusterName` in `InstanceListForm.fillDefaultValue()`** - so when not specified, it stays `null`/blank.
2. **Modify `CatalogServiceV2Impl.listInstances()`** to handle blank/null `clusterName` by not doing the cluster check (and passing it through to `ServiceUtil.selectInstances` which handles it).

Actually, looking at the code flow more carefully:

`InstanceControllerV3.list()` calls `catalogService.listInstances(...)` with `instanceListForm.getClusterName()`.
If we remove the default fill, `clusterName` will be `null`. Then `CatalogServiceV2Impl.listInstances()` will call `serviceStorage.getClusters(service).contains(null)` which returns false, throwing exception.

So we also need to change `CatalogServiceV2Impl.listInstances()` to handle blank/null clusterName.

But also, `InstanceOpenApiController.list()` calls `instanceOperator.listInstance(...)`. The `InstanceOperatorClientImpl.listInstance()` already handles null/blank cluster correctly since it passes it through to `ServiceUtil.selectInstancesWithHealthyProtection()` which handles it via `doSelectInstances()`.

So the fix should be in `CatalogServiceV2Impl.listInstances()` - when `clusterName` is blank, we should skip the cluster check and just use `ServiceUtil.selectInstances` with the blank cluster (which will match all).

Let me write a script to reproduce the issue first, then make the fix.

Actually, let me first check the tests to understand what's expected after the fix:

    46	@ExtendWith(MockitoExtension.class)
    47	class InstanceOpenApiControllerTest {
    48	    
    49	    @Mock
    50	    private InstanceOperator instanceOperator;
    51	    
    52	    @Mock
    53	    private SwitchDomain switchDomain;
    54	    
    55	    private InstanceOpenApiController instanceOpenApiController;
    56	    
    57	    @BeforeEach
    58	    void setUp() {
    59	        instanceOpenApiController = new InstanceOpenApiController(instanceOperator, switchDomain);
    60	    }
    61	    
    62	    @AfterEach
    63	    void tearDown() {
    64	    }
    65	    
    66	    @Test
    67	    void testRegister() throws NacosException {
    68	        InstanceForm instanceForm = new InstanceForm();
    69	        instanceForm.setServiceName("test");
    70	        instanceForm.setIp("1.1.1.1");
    71	        instanceForm.setPort(80);
    72	        Result<String> actual = instanceOpenApiController.register(instanceForm, false);
    73	        verify(instanceOperator).registerInstance(eq(Constants.DEFAULT_NAMESPACE_ID), eq(Constants.DEFAULT_GROUP),
    74	                eq("test"), any(Instance.class));
    75	        assertEquals(ErrorCode.SUCCESS.getCode(), actual.getCode());
    76	        assertEquals(ErrorCode.SUCCESS.getMsg(), actual.getMessage());
    77	        assertEquals("ok", actual.getData());
    78	    }
    79	    
    80	    @Test
    81	    void testRegisterWithHeartBeat() throws NacosException {
    82	        InstanceForm instanceForm = new InstanceForm();
    83	        instanceForm.setServiceName("test");
    84	        instanceForm.setIp("1.1.1.1");
    85	        instanceForm.setPort(80);
    86	        when(instanceOperator.handleBeat(eq(Constants.DEFAULT_NAMESPACE_ID), eq(Constants.DEFAULT_GROUP), eq("test"),
    87	                eq("1.1.1.1"), eq(80), eq(Constants.DEFAULT_CLUSTER_NAME), any(), any())).thenReturn(
    88	                NamingResponseCode.RESOURCE_NOT_FOUND, NamingResponseCode.OK);
    89	        Result<String> actual = instanceOpenApiController.register(instanceForm, true);
    90	        assertEquals(ErrorCode.INSTANCE_NOT_FOUND.getCode(), actual.getCode());
    91	        assertEquals(ErrorCode.INSTANCE_NOT_FOUND.getMsg(), actual.getMessage());
    92	        actual = instanceOpenApiController.register(instanceForm, true);
    93	        assertEquals(ErrorCode.SUCCESS.getCode(), actual.getCode());
    94	        assertEquals(ErrorCode.SUCCESS.getMsg(), actual.getMessage());
    95	        assertEquals("ok", actual.getData());
    96	    }
    97	    
    98	    @Test
    99	    void testDeregister() throws NacosException {
   100	        InstanceForm instanceForm = new InstanceForm();
   101	        instanceForm.setServiceName("test");
   102	        instanceForm.setIp("1.1.1.1");
   103	        instanceForm.setPort(80);
   104	        Result<String> actual = instanceOpenApiController.deregister(instanceForm);
   105	        verify(instanceOperator).removeInstance(eq(Constants.DEFAULT_NAMESPACE_ID), eq(Constants.DEFAULT_GROUP),
   106	                eq("test"), any(Instance.class));
   107	        assertEquals(ErrorCode.SUCCESS.getCode(), actual.getCode());
   108	        assertEquals(ErrorCode.SUCCESS.getMsg(), actual.getMessage());
   109	        assertEquals("ok", actual.getData());
   110	    }
   111	    
   112	    @Test
   113	    void testList() throws Exception {
   114	        InstanceListForm instanceForm = new InstanceListForm();
   115	        instanceForm.setServiceName("test");
   116	        Instance instance = new Instance();
   117	        instance.setIp("1.1.1.1");
   118	        ServiceInfo serviceInfo = new ServiceInfo();
   119	        serviceInfo.setName("test");
   120	        serviceInfo.setHosts(Collections.singletonList(instance));
   121	        when(instanceOperator.listInstance(Constants.DEFAULT_NAMESPACE_ID, Constants.DEFAULT_GROUP, "test", null,
   122	                Constants.DEFAULT_CLUSTER_NAME, false)).thenReturn(serviceInfo);
   123	        Result<List<Instance>> actual = instanceOpenApiController.list(instanceForm);
   124	        assertEquals(ErrorCode.SUCCESS.getCode(), actual.getCode());
   125	        assertEquals(ErrorCode.SUCCESS.getMsg(), actual.getMessage());
   126	        assertEquals(1, actual.getData().size());
   127	        assertEquals("1.1.1.1", actual.getData().get(0).getIp());
   128	    }

Now I need to decide on the fix. The PR description suggests:

1. `InstanceListForm.fillDefaultValue()` should not fill default for `clusterName`, OR
2. `listInstances` should use `listAllInstances` logic when `clusterName` is empty.

Looking at the code paths:

**Path 1 (InstanceControllerV3.list → CatalogServiceV2Impl.listInstances):**
- `InstanceListForm.fillDefaultValue()` sets `clusterName` to "DEFAULT" if blank
- `CatalogServiceV2Impl.listInstances()` does exact cluster match

**Path 2 (InstanceOpenApiController.list → InstanceOperatorClientImpl.listInstance):**
- `InstanceListForm.fillDefaultValue()` sets `clusterName` to "DEFAULT" if blank
- `InstanceOperatorClientImpl.listInstance()` passes cluster to `ServiceUtil.selectInstancesWithHealthyProtection()` which handles empty/blank correctly

So the fix should focus on `CatalogServiceV2Impl.listInstances()`. The simplest fix is to modify `CatalogServiceV2Impl.listInstances()` to handle blank/null `clusterName` by not doing the cluster existence check and passing the cluster through to `ServiceUtil.selectInstances()`.

But we also need to remove the default filling in `InstanceListForm.fillDefaultValue()` because even if we fix `CatalogServiceV2Impl`, filling with "DEFAULT" would still cause the wrong behavior (it would match only instances in "DEFAULT" cluster, not all instances).

Wait, let me re-read the PR description:
> v3 HTTP 路径（有问题）
> InstanceListForm.fillDefaultValue()
>     clusterName 为空 → 填充为 "DEFAULT"               // 强制覆盖

So the problem is that blank clusterName becomes "DEFAULT", and then it tries to find "DEFAULT" cluster which doesn't exist. 

I think both fixes should be applied:
1. Remove the default filling for `clusterName` in `InstanceListForm.fillDefaultValue()` 
2. Fix `CatalogServiceV2Impl.listInstances()` to handle blank/null `clusterName`

Let me now make the changes:

First, let me fix `InstanceListForm.fillDefaultValue()`:

The lines to change are 71-73:
```java
        if (StringUtils.isBlank(clusterName)) {
            clusterName = UtilsAndCommons.DEFAULT_CLUSTER_NAME;
        }
```

These should be removed (or commented out). But we need to be careful - the `InstanceOpenApiControllerTest` line 121-122 expects `Constants.DEFAULT_CLUSTER_NAME`:

```java
when(instanceOperator.listInstance(Constants.DEFAULT_NAMESPACE_ID, Constants.DEFAULT_GROUP, "test", null,
                Constants.DEFAULT_CLUSTER_NAME, false)).thenReturn(serviceInfo);
```

Wait, this test sets no clusterName on the form, so after `fillDefaultValue`, it becomes "DEFAULT". The test expects "DEFAULT" to be passed to `instanceOperator.listInstance`. But the PR description says this is wrong behavior...

The test `testListInstancesNonExistCluster` expects that when a non-existent cluster "DD" is passed, it throws an exception. After the fix, if "DD" is blank/null, it should NOT throw an exception but return all instances. But if "DD" is a non-blank, specific cluster, it should still throw.

OK, I think the right approach is:

1. Remove the default filling for `clusterName` in `InstanceListForm.fillDefaultValue()` - let it stay null/blank when not provided.
2. Modify `CatalogServiceV2Impl.listInstances()` to handle null/blank `clusterName` by not checking cluster existence and passing empty string to `ServiceUtil.selectInstances`.

package com.alibaba.nacos.naming.model.form;

import com.alibaba.nacos.api.common.Constants;
import com.alibaba.nacos.api.exception.api.NacosApiException;
import com.alibaba.nacos.api.model.v2.ErrorCode;
import com.alibaba.nacos.common.utils.StringUtils;
import com.alibaba.nacos.api.model.NacosForm;
import com.alibaba.nacos.naming.misc.UtilsAndCommons;
import org.springframework.http.HttpStatus;

import java.util.Objects;

/**
 * Instance List Form.
 *
 * @author xiweng.yy
 */
public class InstanceListForm implements NacosForm {
    
    private static final long serialVersionUID = -3760300561436525429L;
    
    private String namespaceId;
    
    private String groupName;
    
    private String serviceName;
    
    private String clusterName;
    
    private Boolean healthyOnly;
    
    /**
     * check param.
     *
     * @throws NacosApiException NacosApiException
     */
    public void validate() throws NacosApiException {
        fillDefaultValue();
        if (StringUtils.isBlank(serviceName)) {
            throw new NacosApiException(HttpStatus.BAD_REQUEST.value(), ErrorCode.PARAMETER_MISSING,
                    "Required parameter 'serviceName' type String is not present");
        }
    }
    
    /**
     * fill default value.
     */
    public void fillDefaultValue() {
        if (StringUtils.isBlank(namespaceId)) {
            namespaceId = Constants.DEFAULT_NAMESPACE_ID;
        }
        if (StringUtils.isBlank(groupName)) {
            groupName = Constants.DEFAULT_GROUP;
        }
        if (StringUtils.isBlank(clusterName)) {
            clusterName = UtilsAndCommons.DEFAULT_CLUSTER_NAME;
        }
        if (null == healthyOnly) {
            healthyOnly = false;
        }
    }
    
    public String getNamespaceId() {
        return namespaceId;
    }
    
    public void setNamespaceId(String namespaceId) {
        this.namespaceId = namespaceId;
    }
    
    public String getGroupName() {
        return groupName;
    }
    
    public void setGroupName(String groupName) {
        this.groupName = groupName;
    }
    
    public String getServiceName() {
        return serviceName;
    }
    
    public void setServiceName(String serviceName) {
        this.serviceName = serviceName;
    }
    
    public String getClusterName() {
        return clusterName;
    }
    
    public void setClusterName(String clusterName) {
        this.clusterName = clusterName;
    }
    
    public Boolean getHealthyOnly() {
        return healthyOnly;
    }
    
    public void setHealthyOnly(Boolean healthyOnly) {
        this.healthyOnly = healthyOnly;
    }
    
    @Override
    public boolean equals(Object o) {
        if (this == o) {
            return true;
        }
        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass()) {
            return false;
        }
        InstanceListForm that = (InstanceListForm) o;
        return Objects.equals(namespaceId, that.namespaceId) && Objects.equals(groupName, that.groupName)
                && Objects.equals(serviceName, that.serviceName) && Objects.equals(clusterName, that.clusterName)
                && Objects.equals(healthyOnly, that.healthyOnly);
    }
    
    @Override
    public int hashCode() {
        return Objects.hash(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName, clusterName, healthyOnly);
    }
}

   108	    public Boolean getHealthyOnly() {
   109	        return healthyOnly;
   110	    }
   111	    
   112	    public void setHealthyOnly(Boolean healthyOnly) {
   113	        this.healthyOnly = healthyOnly;
   114	    }
   115	    
   116	    @Override
   117	    public boolean equals(Object o) {
   118	        if (this == o) {
   119	            return true;
   120	        }
   121	        if (o == null || getClass() != o.getClass()) {
   122	            return false;
   123	        }
   124	        InstanceListForm that = (InstanceListForm) o;
   125	        return Objects.equals(namespaceId, that.namespaceId) && Objects.equals(groupName, that.groupName)
   126	                && Objects.equals(serviceName, that.serviceName) && Objects.equals(clusterName, that.clusterName)
   127	                && Objects.equals(healthyOnly, that.healthyOnly);
   128	    }
   129	    
   130	    @Override
   131	    public int hashCode() {
   132	        return Objects.hash(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName, clusterName, healthyOnly);
   133	    }
   134	}

    51	/**
    52	 * Catalog service for v2.x .
    53	 *
    54	 * @author xiweng.yy
    55	 */
    56	@Component()
    57	public class CatalogServiceV2Impl implements CatalogService {
    58	    
    59	    private final ServiceStorage serviceStorage;
    60	    
    61	    private final NamingMetadataManager metadataManager;
    62	    
    63	    private static final int DEFAULT_PORT = 80;
    64	    
    65	    public CatalogServiceV2Impl(ServiceStorage serviceStorage, NamingMetadataManager metadataManager) {
    66	        this.serviceStorage = serviceStorage;
    67	        this.metadataManager = metadataManager;
    68	    }
    69	    
    70	    @Override
    71	    public ServiceDetailInfo getServiceDetail(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName)
    72	            throws NacosException {
    73	        Service service = Service.newService(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName);
    74	        if (!ServiceManager.getInstance().containSingleton(service)) {
    75	            throw new NacosException(NacosException.NOT_FOUND,
    76	                    String.format("service %s@@%s is not found!", groupName, serviceName));
    77	        }
    78	        service = ServiceManager.getInstance().getSingleton(service);
    79	        Optional<ServiceMetadata> metadata = metadataManager.getServiceMetadata(service);
    80	        ServiceMetadata detailedService = metadata.orElseGet(ServiceMetadata::new);
    81	        
    82	        ServiceDetailInfo result = new ServiceDetailInfo();
    83	        result.setNamespaceId(service.getNamespace());
    84	        result.setGroupName(service.getGroup());
    85	        result.setServiceName(serviceName);
    86	        result.setEphemeral(service.isEphemeral());
    87	        result.setProtectThreshold(detailedService.getProtectThreshold());
    88	        result.setSelector(detailedService.getSelector());
    89	        result.setMetadata(detailedService.getExtendData());
    90	        
    91	        Map<String, ClusterInfo> clusters = new HashMap<>(serviceStorage.getClusters(service).size());
    92	        for (String each : serviceStorage.getClusters(service)) {
    93	            ClusterMetadata clusterMetadata =
    94	                    detailedService.getClusters().containsKey(each) ? detailedService.getClusters().get(each)
    95	                            : new ClusterMetadata();
    96	            ClusterInfo clusterInfo = new ClusterInfo();
    97	            clusterInfo.setClusterName(each);
    98	            clusterInfo.setHealthChecker(clusterMetadata.getHealthChecker());
    99	            clusterInfo.setMetadata(clusterMetadata.getExtendData());
   100	            clusterInfo.setUseInstancePortForCheck(clusterMetadata.isUseInstancePortForCheck());
   101	            clusterInfo.setHealthyCheckPort(clusterMetadata.getHealthyCheckPort());
   102	            clusters.put(each, clusterInfo);
   103	        }
   104	        result.setClusterMap(clusters);
   105	        return result;
   106	    }
   107	    
   108	    @Override
   109	    public List<? extends Instance> listInstances(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName,
   110	            String clusterName) throws NacosException {
   111	        Service service = Service.newService(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName);
   112	        if (!ServiceManager.getInstance().containSingleton(service)) {
   113	            throw new NacosException(NacosException.NOT_FOUND,
   114	                    String.format("service %s@@%s is not found!", groupName, serviceName));
   115	        }
   116	        if (!serviceStorage.getClusters(service).contains(clusterName)) {
   117	            throw new NacosException(NacosException.NOT_FOUND, "cluster " + clusterName + " is not found!");
   118	        }
   119	        ServiceInfo serviceInfo = serviceStorage.getData(service);
   120	        ServiceInfo result = ServiceUtil.selectInstances(serviceInfo, clusterName);
   121	        return result.getHosts();
   122	    }
   123	    
   124	    @Override
   125	    public List<? extends Instance> listAllInstances(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName) {
   126	        Service service = Service.newService(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName);
   127	        if (!ServiceManager.getInstance().containSingleton(service)) {
   128	            return Collections.EMPTY_LIST;
   129	        }
   130	        
   131	        ServiceInfo serviceInfo = serviceStorage.getData(service);
   132	        
   133	        return serviceInfo.getHosts();
   134	    }
   135	    
   136	    @Override
   137	    public Object pageListService(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName, int pageNo, int pageSize,
   138	            String instancePattern, boolean ignoreEmptyService) throws NacosException {
   139	        ObjectNode result = JacksonUtils.createEmptyJsonNode();
   140	        List<ServiceView> serviceViews = new LinkedList<>();
   141	        Collection<Service> services = patternServices(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName);
   142	        if (ignoreEmptyService) {
   143	            services = services.stream().filter(each -> 0 != serviceStorage.getData(each).ipCount())
   144	                    .collect(Collectors.toList());
   145	        }
   146	        result.put(FieldsConstants.COUNT, services.size());
   147	        services = doPage(services, pageNo - 1, pageSize);
   148	        for (Service each : services) {
   149	            ServiceMetadata serviceMetadata = metadataManager.getServiceMetadata(each).orElseGet(ServiceMetadata::new);
   150	            ServiceView serviceView = new ServiceView();
   151	            serviceView.setName(each.getName());
   152	            serviceView.setGroupName(each.getGroup());
   153	            serviceView.setClusterCount(serviceStorage.getClusters(each).size());
   154	            serviceView.setIpCount(serviceStorage.getData(each).ipCount());
   155	            serviceView.setHealthyInstanceCount(countHealthyInstance(serviceStorage.getData(each)));
   156	            serviceView.setTriggerFlag(isProtectThreshold(serviceView, serviceMetadata) ? "true" : "false");
   157	            serviceViews.add(serviceView);
   158	        }
   159	        result.set(FieldsConstants.SERVICE_LIST, JacksonUtils.transferToJsonNode(serviceViews));
   160	        return result;
   161	    }
   162	    
   163	    @Override
   164	    public Page<ServiceView> listService(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName, int pageNo,
   165	            int pageSize, boolean ignoreEmptyService) throws NacosException {
   166	        Page<ServiceView> serviceViews = new Page<>();
   167	        Collection<Service> services = patternServices(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName);
   168	        if (ignoreEmptyService) {
   169	            services = services.stream().filter(each -> 0 != serviceStorage.getData(each).ipCount()).toList();
   170	        }
   171	        Page<Service> page = PageUtil.subPage(services.stream().toList(), pageNo, pageSize);
   172	        serviceViews.setTotalCount(page.getTotalCount());
   173	        serviceViews.setPageNumber(page.getPageNumber());
   174	        serviceViews.setPagesAvailable(page.getPagesAvailable());
   175	        for (Service each : page.getPageItems()) {
   176	            ServiceMetadata serviceMetadata = metadataManager.getServiceMetadata(each).orElseGet(ServiceMetadata::new);
   177	            ServiceView serviceView = new ServiceView();
   178	            serviceView.setName(each.getName());
   179	            serviceView.setGroupName(each.getGroup());
   180	            serviceView.setClusterCount(serviceStorage.getClusters(each).size());
   181	            serviceView.setIpCount(serviceStorage.getData(each).ipCount());
   182	            serviceView.setHealthyInstanceCount(countHealthyInstance(serviceStorage.getData(each)));
   183	            serviceView.setTriggerFlag(isProtectThreshold(serviceView, serviceMetadata) ? "true" : "false");
   184	            serviceViews.getPageItems().add(serviceView);
   185	        }
   186	        return serviceViews;
   187	    }
   188	    
   189	    private int countHealthyInstance(ServiceInfo data) {
   190	        int result = 0;
   191	        for (Instance each : data.getHosts()) {
   192	            if (each.isHealthy()) {
   193	                result++;
   194	            }
   195	        }
   196	        return result;
   197	    }
   198	    
   199	    private boolean isProtectThreshold(ServiceView serviceView, ServiceMetadata metadata) {
   200	        return (serviceView.getHealthyInstanceCount() * 1.0 / serviceView.getIpCount())
   201	                <= metadata.getProtectThreshold();
   202	    }
   203	    
   204	    @Override
   205	    public Page<ServiceDetailInfo> pageListServiceDetail(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName,
   206	            int pageNo, int pageSize) throws NacosException {
   207	        Collection<Service> services = patternServices(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName);
   208	        Page<Service> servicePage = PageUtil.subPage(services.stream().toList(), pageNo, pageSize);
   209	        Page<ServiceDetailInfo> result = new Page<>();
   210	        result.setPagesAvailable(servicePage.getPagesAvailable());
   211	        result.setPageNumber(servicePage.getPageNumber());
   212	        result.setTotalCount(servicePage.getTotalCount());
   213	        List<ServiceDetailInfo> pagedItem = new LinkedList<>();
   214	        for (Service each : servicePage.getPageItems()) {
   215	            ServiceDetailInfo serviceDetailInfo = new ServiceDetailInfo();
   216	            serviceDetailInfo.setServiceName(each.getName());
   217	            serviceDetailInfo.setGroupName(each.getGroup());
   218	            ServiceMetadata serviceMetadata = metadataManager.getServiceMetadata(each).orElseGet(ServiceMetadata::new);
   219	            serviceDetailInfo.setMetadata(serviceMetadata.getExtendData());
   220	            serviceDetailInfo.setClusterMap(getClusterMap(each));
   221	            pagedItem.add(serviceDetailInfo);
   222	        }
   223	        result.setPageItems(pagedItem);
   224	        return result;
   225	    }
   226	    
   227	    private Map<String, ClusterInfo> getClusterMap(Service service) {
   228	        Map<String, ClusterInfo> result = new HashMap<>(1);
   229	        for (Instance each : serviceStorage.getData(service).getHosts()) {
   230	            if (!result.containsKey(each.getClusterName())) {
   231	                ClusterInfo clusterInfo = new ClusterInfo();
   232	                clusterInfo.setHosts(new LinkedList<>());
   233	                result.put(each.getClusterName(), clusterInfo);
   234	            }
   235	            result.get(each.getClusterName()).getHosts().add(each);
   236	        }
   237	        return result;
   238	    }
   239	    
   240	    private Collection<Service> patternServices(String namespaceId, String group, String serviceName) {
   241	        boolean noFilter = StringUtils.isBlank(serviceName) && StringUtils.isBlank(group);
   242	        if (noFilter) {
   243	            return ServiceManager.getInstance().getSingletons(namespaceId);
   244	        }
   245	        Collection<Service> result = new LinkedList<>();
   246	        StringJoiner regex = new StringJoiner(Constants.SERVICE_INFO_SPLITER);
   247	        regex.add(getRegexString(group));
   248	        regex.add(getRegexString(serviceName));
   249	        String regexString = regex.toString();
   250	        for (Service each : ServiceManager.getInstance().getSingletons(namespaceId)) {
   251	            if (each.getGroupedServiceName().matches(regexString)) {
   252	                result.add(each);
   253	            }
   254	        }
   255	        return result;
   256	    }
   257	    
   258	    private String getRegexString(String target) {
   259	        return StringUtils.isBlank(target) ? Constants.ANY_PATTERN
   260	                : Constants.ANY_PATTERN + target + Constants.ANY_PATTERN;
   261	    }
   262	    
   263	    private Collection<Service> doPage(Collection<Service> services, int pageNo, int pageSize) {
   264	        if (pageNo == 0 && services.size() < pageSize) {
   265	            return services;
   266	        }
   267	        int start = pageNo * pageSize;
   268	        if (start > services.size()) {
   269	            return Collections.emptyList();
   270	        }
   271	        Collection<Service> result = new LinkedList<>();
   272	        int i = 0;
   273	        for (Service each : services) {
   274	            if (i++ < start) {
   275	                continue;
   276	            }
   277	            result.add(each);
   278	            if (result.size() >= pageSize) {
   279	                break;
   280	            }
   281	        }
   282	        return result;
   283	    }
   284	}

    51	/**
    52	 * Catalog service for v2.x .
    53	 *
    54	 * @author xiweng.yy
    55	 */
    56	@Component()
    57	public class CatalogServiceV2Impl implements CatalogService {
    58	    
    59	    private final ServiceStorage serviceStorage;
    60	    
    61	    private final NamingMetadataManager metadataManager;
    62	    
    63	    private static final int DEFAULT_PORT = 80;
    64	    
    65	    public CatalogServiceV2Impl(ServiceStorage serviceStorage, NamingMetadataManager metadataManager) {
    66	        this.serviceStorage = serviceStorage;
    67	        this.metadataManager = metadataManager;
    68	    }
    69	    
    70	    @Override
    71	    public ServiceDetailInfo getServiceDetail(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName)
    72	            throws NacosException {
    73	        Service service = Service.newService(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName);
    74	        if (!ServiceManager.getInstance().containSingleton(service)) {
    75	            throw new NacosException(NacosException.NOT_FOUND,
    76	                    String.format("service %s@@%s is not found!", groupName, serviceName));
    77	        }
    78	        service = ServiceManager.getInstance().getSingleton(service);
    79	        Optional<ServiceMetadata> metadata = metadataManager.getServiceMetadata(service);
    80	        ServiceMetadata detailedService = metadata.orElseGet(ServiceMetadata::new);
    81	        
    82	        ServiceDetailInfo result = new ServiceDetailInfo();
    83	        result.setNamespaceId(service.getNamespace());
    84	        result.setGroupName(service.getGroup());
    85	        result.setServiceName(serviceName);
    86	        result.setEphemeral(service.isEphemeral());
    87	        result.setProtectThreshold(detailedService.getProtectThreshold());
    88	        result.setSelector(detailedService.getSelector());
    89	        result.setMetadata(detailedService.getExtendData());
    90	        
    91	        Map<String, ClusterInfo> clusters = new HashMap<>(serviceStorage.getClusters(service).size());
    92	        for (String each : serviceStorage.getClusters(service)) {
    93	            ClusterMetadata clusterMetadata =
    94	                    detailedService.getClusters().containsKey(each) ? detailedService.getClusters().get(each)
    95	                            : new ClusterMetadata();
    96	            ClusterInfo clusterInfo = new ClusterInfo();
    97	            clusterInfo.setClusterName(each);
    98	            clusterInfo.setHealthChecker(clusterMetadata.getHealthChecker());
    99	            clusterInfo.setMetadata(clusterMetadata.getExtendData());
   100	            clusterInfo.setUseInstancePortForCheck(clusterMetadata.isUseInstancePortForCheck());
   101	            clusterInfo.setHealthyCheckPort(clusterMetadata.getHealthyCheckPort());
   102	            clusters.put(each, clusterInfo);
   103	        }
   104	        result.setClusterMap(clusters);
   105	        return result;
   106	    }
   107	    
   108	    @Override
   109	    public List<? extends Instance> listInstances(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName,
   110	            String clusterName) throws NacosException {
   111	        Service service = Service.newService(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName);
   112	        if (!ServiceManager.getInstance().containSingleton(service)) {
   113	            throw new NacosException(NacosException.NOT_FOUND,
   114	                    String.format("service %s@@%s is not found!", groupName, serviceName));
   115	        }
   116	        if (StringUtils.isNotBlank(clusterName) && !serviceStorage.getClusters(service).contains(clusterName)) {
   117	            throw new NacosException(NacosException.NOT_FOUND, "cluster " + clusterName + " is not found!");
   118	        }
   119	        ServiceInfo serviceInfo = serviceStorage.getData(service);
   120	        ServiceInfo result = ServiceUtil.selectInstances(serviceInfo, StringUtils.isBlank(clusterName) ? StringUtils.EMPTY : clusterName);
   121	        return result.getHosts();
   122	    }
   123	    
   124	    @Override
   125	    public List<? extends Instance> listAllInstances(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName) {
   126	        Service service = Service.newService(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName);
   127	        if (!ServiceManager.getInstance().containSingleton(service)) {
   128	            return Collections.EMPTY_LIST;
   129	        }
   130	        
   131	        ServiceInfo serviceInfo = serviceStorage.getData(service);
   132	        
   133	        return serviceInfo.getHosts();
   134	    }
   135	    
   136	    @Override
   137	    public Object pageListService(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName, int pageNo, int pageSize,
   138	            String instancePattern, boolean ignoreEmptyService) throws NacosException {
   139	        ObjectNode result = JacksonUtils.createEmptyJsonNode();
   140	        List<ServiceView> serviceViews = new LinkedList<>();
   141	        Collection<Service> services = patternServices(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName);
   142	        if (ignoreEmptyService) {
   143	            services = services.stream().filter(each -> 0 != serviceStorage.getData(each).ipCount())
   144	                    .collect(Collectors.toList());
   145	        }
   146	        result.put(FieldsConstants.COUNT, services.size());
   147	        services = doPage(services, pageNo - 1, pageSize);
   148	        for (Service each : services) {
   149	            ServiceMetadata serviceMetadata = metadataManager.getServiceMetadata(each).orElseGet(ServiceMetadata::new);
   150	            ServiceView serviceView = new ServiceView();
   151	            serviceView.setName(each.getName());
   152	            serviceView.setGroupName(each.getGroup());
   153	            serviceView.setClusterCount(serviceStorage.getClusters(each).size());
   154	            serviceView.setIpCount(serviceStorage.getData(each).ipCount());
   155	            serviceView.setHealthyInstanceCount(countHealthyInstance(serviceStorage.getData(each)));
   156	            serviceView.setTriggerFlag(isProtectThreshold(serviceView, serviceMetadata) ? "true" : "false");
   157	            serviceViews.add(serviceView);
   158	        }
   159	        result.set(FieldsConstants.SERVICE_LIST, JacksonUtils.transferToJsonNode(serviceViews));
   160	        return result;
   161	    }
   162	    
   163	    @Override
   164	    public Page<ServiceView> listService(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName, int pageNo,
   165	            int pageSize, boolean ignoreEmptyService) throws NacosException {
   166	        Page<ServiceView> serviceViews = new Page<>();
   167	        Collection<Service> services = patternServices(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName);
   168	        if (ignoreEmptyService) {
   169	            services = services.stream().filter(each -> 0 != serviceStorage.getData(each).ipCount()).toList();
   170	        }
   171	        Page<Service> page = PageUtil.subPage(services.stream().toList(), pageNo, pageSize);
   172	        serviceViews.setTotalCount(page.getTotalCount());
   173	        serviceViews.setPageNumber(page.getPageNumber());
   174	        serviceViews.setPagesAvailable(page.getPagesAvailable());
   175	        for (Service each : page.getPageItems()) {
   176	            ServiceMetadata serviceMetadata = metadataManager.getServiceMetadata(each).orElseGet(ServiceMetadata::new);
   177	            ServiceView serviceView = new ServiceView();
   178	            serviceView.setName(each.getName());
   179	            serviceView.setGroupName(each.getGroup());
   180	            serviceView.setClusterCount(serviceStorage.getClusters(each).size());
   181	            serviceView.setIpCount(serviceStorage.getData(each).ipCount());
   182	            serviceView.setHealthyInstanceCount(countHealthyInstance(serviceStorage.getData(each)));
   183	            serviceView.setTriggerFlag(isProtectThreshold(serviceView, serviceMetadata) ? "true" : "false");
   184	            serviceViews.getPageItems().add(serviceView);
   185	        }
   186	        return serviceViews;
   187	    }
   188	    
   189	    private int countHealthyInstance(ServiceInfo data) {
   190	        int result = 0;
   191	        for (Instance each : data.getHosts()) {
   192	            if (each.isHealthy()) {
   193	                result++;
   194	            }
   195	        }
   196	        return result;
   197	    }
   198	    
   199	    private boolean isProtectThreshold(ServiceView serviceView, ServiceMetadata metadata) {
   200	        return (serviceView.getHealthyInstanceCount() * 1.0 / serviceView.getIpCount())
   201	                <= metadata.getProtectThreshold();
   202	    }
   203	    
   204	    @Override
   205	    public Page<ServiceDetailInfo> pageListServiceDetail(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName,
   206	            int pageNo, int pageSize) throws NacosException {
   207	        Collection<Service> services = patternServices(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName);
   208	        Page<Service> servicePage = PageUtil.subPage(services.stream().toList(), pageNo, pageSize);
   209	        Page<ServiceDetailInfo> result = new Page<>();
   210	        result.setPagesAvailable(servicePage.getPagesAvailable());
   211	        result.setPageNumber(servicePage.getPageNumber());
   212	        result.setTotalCount(servicePage.getTotalCount());
   213	        List<ServiceDetailInfo> pagedItem = new LinkedList<>();
   214	        for (Service each : servicePage.getPageItems()) {
   215	            ServiceDetailInfo serviceDetailInfo = new ServiceDetailInfo();
   216	            serviceDetailInfo.setServiceName(each.getName());
   217	            serviceDetailInfo.setGroupName(each.getGroup());
   218	            ServiceMetadata serviceMetadata = metadataManager.getServiceMetadata(each).orElseGet(ServiceMetadata::new);
   219	            serviceDetailInfo.setMetadata(serviceMetadata.getExtendData());
   220	            serviceDetailInfo.setClusterMap(getClusterMap(each));
   221	            pagedItem.add(serviceDetailInfo);
   222	        }
   223	        result.setPageItems(pagedItem);
   224	        return result;
   225	    }
   226	    
   227	    private Map<String, ClusterInfo> getClusterMap(Service service) {
   228	        Map<String, ClusterInfo> result = new HashMap<>(1);
   229	        for (Instance each : serviceStorage.getData(service).getHosts()) {
   230	            if (!result.containsKey(each.getClusterName())) {
   231	                ClusterInfo clusterInfo = new ClusterInfo();
   232	                clusterInfo.setHosts(new LinkedList<>());
   233	                result.put(each.getClusterName(), clusterInfo);
   234	            }
   235	            result.get(each.getClusterName()).getHosts().add(each);
   236	        }
   237	        return result;
   238	    }
   239	    
   240	    private Collection<Service> patternServices(String namespaceId, String group, String serviceName) {
   241	        boolean noFilter = StringUtils.isBlank(serviceName) && StringUtils.isBlank(group);
   242	        if (noFilter) {
   243	            return ServiceManager.getInstance().getSingletons(namespaceId);
   244	        }
   245	        Collection<Service> result = new LinkedList<>();
   246	        StringJoiner regex = new StringJoiner(Constants.SERVICE_INFO_SPLITER);
   247	        regex.add(getRegexString(group));
   248	        regex.add(getRegexString(serviceName));
   249	        String regexString = regex.toString();
   250	        for (Service each : ServiceManager.getInstance().getSingletons(namespaceId)) {
   251	            if (each.getGroupedServiceName().matches(regexString)) {
   252	                result.add(each);
   253	            }
   254	        }
   255	        return result;
   256	    }
   257	    
   258	    private String getRegexString(String target) {
   259	        return StringUtils.isBlank(target) ? Constants.ANY_PATTERN
   260	                : Constants.ANY_PATTERN + target + Constants.ANY_PATTERN;
   261	    }
   262	    
   263	    private Collection<Service> doPage(Collection<Service> services, int pageNo, int pageSize) {
   264	        if (pageNo == 0 && services.size() < pageSize) {
   265	            return services;
   266	        }
   267	        int start = pageNo * pageSize;
   268	        if (start > services.size()) {
   269	            return Collections.emptyList();
   270	        }
   271	        Collection<Service> result = new LinkedList<>();
   272	        int i = 0;
   273	        for (Service each : services) {
   274	            if (i++ < start) {
   275	                continue;
   276	            }
   277	            result.add(each);
   278	            if (result.size() >= pageSize) {
   279	                break;
   280	            }
   281	        }
   282	        return result;
   283	    }
   284	}

    27	/**
    28	 * Catalog service.
    29	 *
    30	 * @author xiweng.yy
    31	 */
    32	public interface CatalogService {
    33	    
    34	    /**
    35	     * Get service detail information.
    36	     *
    37	     * @param namespaceId namespace id of service
    38	     * @param groupName   group name of service
    39	     * @param serviceName service name
    40	     * @return detail information of service
    41	     * @throws NacosException exception in query
    42	     */
    43	    ServiceDetailInfo getServiceDetail(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName) throws NacosException;
    44	    
    45	    /**
    46	     * List all instances of specified services.
    47	     *
    48	     * @param namespaceId namespace id of service
    49	     * @param groupName   group name of service
    50	     * @param serviceName service name
    51	     * @param clusterName cluster name of instances
    52	     * @return instances page object
    53	     * @throws NacosException exception in query
    54	     */
    55	    List<? extends Instance> listInstances(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName, String clusterName)
    56	            throws NacosException;
    57	    
    58	    /**
    59	     * List all instances of specified services.
    60	     *
    61	     * @param namespaceId namespace id of service
    62	     * @param groupName   group name of service
    63	     * @param serviceName service name
    64	     * @return instances list
    65	     */
    66	    List<? extends Instance> listAllInstances(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName);
    67	    
    68	    /**
    69	     * List service by page.
    70	     *
    71	     * @param namespaceId        namespace id of service
    72	     * @param groupName          group name of service
    73	     * @param serviceName        service name
    74	     * @param pageNo             page number
    75	     * @param pageSize           page size
    76	     * @param instancePattern    contained instances pattern
    77	     * @param ignoreEmptyService whether ignore empty service
    78	     * @return service list
    79	     * @throws NacosException exception in query
    80	     * @deprecated after v1 http api removed, use {@link #listService(String, String, String, int, int, boolean)} replace.
    81	     */

    48

    50

    58	        this.instanceServiceV2 = instanceServiceV2;
    59	    }
    60	    
    61	    @Override
    62	    public Page<? extends Instance> listInstances(String namespaceId, String serviceNameWithoutGroup, String groupName,
    63	            String clusterName, int page, int pageSize) throws NacosException {
    64	        List<? extends Instance> instances = catalogService.listInstances(namespaceId, groupName,
    65	                serviceNameWithoutGroup, clusterName);
    66	        return PageUtil.subPage(instances, page, pageSize);
    67	    }

- `instanceOperator.listInstance("public", "DEFAULT_GROUP", "test", null, null, false)`

Actually, the user said "Your task is to make the minimal changes to non-tests files in the directory to ensure the <pr_description> is satisfied." So I should only modify non-test files. The test failure is expected since the behavior has changed.

But wait, let me reconsider the approach. Maybe instead of removing the `fillDefaultValue` for clusterName entirely, we should keep it but also fix `CatalogServiceV2Impl.listInstances()`. Let me think about this more carefully.

The PR description says:
> 修复方式是 InstanceListForm.fillDefaultValue() 不应该对 clusterName 做默认填充，或者 listInstances 里 clusterName 为空时走 listAllInstances 的逻辑。

Two approaches:
1. `InstanceListForm.fillDefaultValue()` should NOT fill default for `clusterName`
2. OR in `listInstances`, when `clusterName` is empty, use `listAllInstances` logic

I went with approach 1 + fixing `listInstances` to handle blank clusterName. But approach 2 alone might be sufficient and would not break the test that expects "DEFAULT".

Let me reconsider: What if I revert the `InstanceListForm` change and only fix `CatalogServiceV2Impl.listInstances()`? 

If we keep `fillDefaultValue` setting clusterName to "DEFAULT", then the call goes to `listInstances` with "DEFAULT". With our fix to `listInstances`:
- `StringUtils.isNotBlank("DEFAULT")` is true
- `serviceStorage.getClusters(service).contains("DEFAULT")` — if "DEFAULT" is not a cluster, throws exception

So approach 2 alone would NOT fix the issue. The problem is that "DEFAULT" gets matched exactly against actual cluster names.

So actually, we need both fixes:
1. Don't fill "DEFAULT" for clusterName (let it be null/blank)
2. Handle null/blank in `listInstances`

OR, we could do approach 2 differently: when clusterName is "DEFAULT" (or blank), call `listAllInstances` logic instead. But "DEFAULT" is a valid cluster name that some users might use. So treating "DEFAULT" specially would be wrong.

I think the correct fix IS to remove the default filling AND fix `listInstances` to handle blank. The test needs to be updated accordingly.

But the user said not to modify tests. Let me check if there's a way the test could still pass...

    51	/**
    52	 * Catalog service for v2.x .
    53	 *
    54	 * @author xiweng.yy
    55	 */
    56	@Component()
    57	public class CatalogServiceV2Impl implements CatalogService {
    58	    
    59	    private final ServiceStorage serviceStorage;
    60	    
    61	    private final NamingMetadataManager metadataManager;
    62	    
    63	    private static final int DEFAULT_PORT = 80;
    64	    
    65	    public CatalogServiceV2Impl(ServiceStorage serviceStorage, NamingMetadataManager metadataManager) {
    66	        this.serviceStorage = serviceStorage;
    67	        this.metadataManager = metadataManager;
    68	    }
    69	    
    70	    @Override
    71	    public ServiceDetailInfo getServiceDetail(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName)
    72	            throws NacosException {
    73	        Service service = Service.newService(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName);
    74	        if (!ServiceManager.getInstance().containSingleton(service)) {
    75	            throw new NacosException(NacosException.NOT_FOUND,
    76	                    String.format("service %s@@%s is not found!", groupName, serviceName));
    77	        }
    78	        service = ServiceManager.getInstance().getSingleton(service);
    79	        Optional<ServiceMetadata> metadata = metadataManager.getServiceMetadata(service);
    80	        ServiceMetadata detailedService = metadata.orElseGet(ServiceMetadata::new);
    81	        
    82	        ServiceDetailInfo result = new ServiceDetailInfo();
    83	        result.setNamespaceId(service.getNamespace());
    84	        result.setGroupName(service.getGroup());
    85	        result.setServiceName(serviceName);
    86	        result.setEphemeral(service.isEphemeral());
    87	        result.setProtectThreshold(detailedService.getProtectThreshold());
    88	        result.setSelector(detailedService.getSelector());
    89	        result.setMetadata(detailedService.getExtendData());
    90	        
    91	        Map<String, ClusterInfo> clusters = new HashMap<>(serviceStorage.getClusters(service).size());
    92	        for (String each : serviceStorage.getClusters(service)) {
    93	            ClusterMetadata clusterMetadata =
    94	                    detailedService.getClusters().containsKey(each) ? detailedService.getClusters().get(each)
    95	                            : new ClusterMetadata();
    96	            ClusterInfo clusterInfo = new ClusterInfo();
    97	            clusterInfo.setClusterName(each);
    98	            clusterInfo.setHealthChecker(clusterMetadata.getHealthChecker());
    99	            clusterInfo.setMetadata(clusterMetadata.getExtendData());
   100	            clusterInfo.setUseInstancePortForCheck(clusterMetadata.isUseInstancePortForCheck());
   101	            clusterInfo.setHealthyCheckPort(clusterMetadata.getHealthyCheckPort());
   102	            clusters.put(each, clusterInfo);
   103	        }
   104	        result.setClusterMap(clusters);
   105	        return result;
   106	    }
   107	    
   108	    @Override
   109	    public List<? extends Instance> listInstances(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName,
   110	            String clusterName) throws NacosException {
   111	        Service service = Service.newService(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName);
   112	        if (!ServiceManager.getInstance().containSingleton(service)) {
   113	            throw new NacosException(NacosException.NOT_FOUND,
   114	                    String.format("service %s@@%s is not found!", groupName, serviceName));
   115	        }
   116	        if (StringUtils.isNotBlank(clusterName) && !serviceStorage.getClusters(service).contains(clusterName)) {
   117	            throw new NacosException(NacosException.NOT_FOUND, "cluster " + clusterName + " is not found!");
   118	        }
   119	        ServiceInfo serviceInfo = serviceStorage.getData(service);
   120	        ServiceInfo result = ServiceUtil.selectInstances(serviceInfo, StringUtils.isBlank(clusterName) ? StringUtils.EMPTY : clusterName);
   121	        return result.getHosts();
   122	    }
   123	    
   124	    @Override
   125	    public List<? extends Instance> listAllInstances(String namespaceId, String groupName, String serviceName) {

```java
public Result<List<? extends Instance>> list(InstanceListForm instanceListForm) throws NacosException {

    }
```

1. `catalogService.listInstances(...)` with blank clusterName → `ServiceUtil.selectInstances(serviceInfo, "")` → returns all instances (no cluster filter)

```java
public Result<List<Instance>> list(InstanceListForm instanceForm) throws Exception {
    instanceForm.validate();
    String namespaceId = instanceForm.getNamespaceId();
    String groupName = instanceForm.getGroupName();
    String serviceName = instanceForm.getServiceName();
    ServiceInfo serviceInfo = instanceOperator.listInstance(namespaceId, groupName, serviceName, null,
            instanceForm.getClusterName(), false);
    return Result.success(serviceInfo.getHosts());
}
```

This passes `clusterName` to `instanceOperator.listInstance()` which goes to `InstanceOperatorClientImpl.listInstance()` → `ServiceUtil.selectInstancesWithHealthyProtection()` → `ServiceUtil.doSelectInstances()`. This already handles null/blank cluster correctly.
